Austrian Coup and the Future of Europe (Part 1) - Lieshan - European Correspondence

Ever since the two national socialist parties came to power, a popular saying has been circulating in European society, saying that if Hitler exists, Europe will be destroyed. This can also prove that the time has reached the eve of the storm. War premonitions are causing anxiety everywhere. Various peace movements are not only under legal pressure, but their significance is also fundamentally denied in terms of public opinion. The wings of the god of war have already spread across the European continent. Anyone who advocates for peace will be told that they are a fool and to stop dreaming and see what era this is. Anyone who opposes war is simply a rebel. Buzzing, swaggering, and neck-craning military reservists are increasing every day and can be encountered everywhere. A somber atmosphere fills the entire Europe, and everything is being pulled back to the state before the European war.

The main protagonists in this are inseparable from the long-standing feud between Germany and France, and the Franco-Italian rivalry for hegemony on the European continent. Germany and Italy seem to be consistent in theory, but in reality, they are wary of each other. This complex triangular situation also includes Britain's clever diplomacy, never allowing one power to dominate the European continent, and a group of supporting actors, such as Poland and the Little Entente, playing roles for their own interests. Forming alliances and conspiracies, vertical and horizontal maneuvering, everything is available in every color and shape. The first line of fire, diplomatic war, is actually also political and economic war, starting in Austria.

This time, the Austrian coup, by a government that had already implemented dictatorship, went a step further and abandoned even the facade of democratic politics, establishing a genuine, authentic Fascist regime (although Dollfuss himself has repeatedly denied it). This fully demonstrates the complex European politics, including France, Germany, Italy, Britain, and various small countries, not only engaging in behind-the-scenes scheming, but also reaching the point of engaging in hand-to-hand combat. An Austrian newspaper said that the Austrian coup was a matter of life and death for them. In fact, it is not just Austria; in a certain sense, it may even be the entire of Europe.

The brotherly bond between Germany and Austria, which is what both Germans and Austrians, especially the German side, have been advocating for, is the memory in the dreams of the Germans, namely, the merger of Germany and Austria to realize the ideal of a Greater Germany. However, this move is enough to make France nervous. Therefore, in this regard, France's foreign policy has never been easily let go. France loudly advocates upholding the balance of power that has already been established in Europe and vigorously monitors Germany's actions. However, Germany's ambitions will never stop halfway. With the emergence of Hitler, what had been going on in secret has been transformed into a clear-cut policy, loudly proclaiming the merger of Germany and Austria. At this point, the atmosphere in Europe suddenly became even more tense.

Mussolini once said that Fascism has no exit. This has two layers of meaning. First, Fascism is extreme nationalism, and fundamentally there is no room for international cooperation. Second, the real deal is still just Mussolini's family, with no other branches. From this, we can understand why Italy and Germany not only cannot act in unison, but also have conflicting views on the Austrian issue. From Italy's own perspective, what it is most worried about is France, but Italy is also very wary of Germany, especially on the Austrian issue. If Austria merges with Germany, another Greater Germanic monster will emerge, which is also something Italy is extremely worried about. Italy's only ambition is to form an alliance with Austria and Hungary, creating its own superior power on the European continent. To this end, it does not hesitate to secretly seduce Austria, preventing Austria from becoming a possession of Germany. In this German-Austrian conflict, Italy is playing more tricks behind the scenes than anyone else, although, on the surface, it pretends to be a mediator.

Since the European War, Austria's status has plummeted. As a result of losing territory and paying reparations, the development of industrial and agricultural areas is unbalanced, and production and consumption often suffer from the inability to distribute them evenly. The population is only over six million, with Vienna alone accounting for more than two million. Therefore, when the world economic panic came, Austria was the first to encounter it and suffer the most. Although Austria has deep ties with Germany in many aspects, especially in terms of history, geography, and race, considering the economic issues, which Germany cannot resolve for Austria, is enough to make figures like Dollfuss resolutely break with Germany and lean towards France, Italy, and other countries, for the sake of the future of the entire country. This is what we cannot forget. Austria's purpose is to find a way to borrow some money economically to restore the country's economy. However, taking advantage of this opportunity, France, Italy, and other countries pulled Austria over, and Austria immediately separated from Germany. This is the inside story of the German-Austrian conflict this time.

The external environment is so complex that the Austrian government authorities are struggling to cope with it, while the domestic parties and political opinions are even more divided. Simply put, the Austrian political parties in the past can be divided into left and right wings. The left wing includes the Social Democratic Party and the Communist Party, and the right wing includes the Christian Social Party (Catholic Party), the Farmers' League, and the Royalist Party. A separate faction is the Austrian National Socialist Party, later led by a specially designated Hitler. The Austrian parliament has a total of 165 members. Except for the relatively weak Communist Party, the Social Democratic Party accounts for a majority of 72 members. Their disadvantage is that there are many factions within the left wing, and opinions are divided. On the common front, the attitude often cannot be consistent. As a result, the smaller right wing takes advantage of it and eventually suffers a complete defeat. Its fate is similar to that of the German Social Democratic Party, but the situation seems even more tragic. Although it is also making strenuous efforts at this moment, it is already too late. Vienna, known as the socialist city, will undoubtedly be greatly tarnished from now on.

Among the right-wing parties, the Christian Social Party is the strongest, occupying 66 members. In principle, it absolutely supports the Dollfuss government. The leader of the Farmers' League, such as former Deputy Prime Minister Winkler, is a person who advocates maintaining the democratic system, especially party politics. Although he is not opposed to organizing a strong government, he is opposed to Fascism. The leader of the Royalist Party, such as the young Prince Starhemberg, is an open advocate of Fascism. He is not only very close to Mussolini, but also has a tacit understanding with Hitler (he participated in Hitler's riots in 1923 while studying at a German star school). He hopes to restore the monarchy and then implement Fascism. Dollfuss himself is between the two mentioned above. For the needs of Austria, he resolutely decided to oppose Hitler. He used the slogan of the party to organize a "Fatherland Front," a semi-military organization. At this moment, he is using this organization as the basis for forming his own dictatorial government.

After July and August this year, the conflict between Germany and Austria obviously became more serious, and the domestic situation also became increasingly complex. The Dollfuss coalition government felt overwhelmed in dealing with it. Although military dictatorship has been implemented, and all powers are in the hands of the security commander or the police chief, the activities of the National Socialist Party are severely suppressed. It is expressly ordered that anyone wearing a swastika badge or singing a National Socialist Party song will be punished with six weeks of imprisonment or a fine of 2,000 schillings (approximately more than 1,000 Chinese currency). At the same time, every effort is being made to search for active members of the National Socialist Party. At the same time, efforts are being made to publicize through leaflets, pamphlets, wall newspapers, announcements, speeches, etc., and vigorously announce the treasonous behavior of the National Socialist Party. The wording seems to be very extreme, for example, calling the National Socialist Party a "contagious disease," "brown plague," or "German-style Communist Party," creating another kind of atmosphere in society, that is, all National Socialists are generally recognized as immoral scoundrels, and Austrian heroes are those who belong to the "Fatherland Front" or "Defense League" and other groups. The efforts of the Dollfuss government have obviously achieved considerable success in this regard, but they have not yet fundamentally solved the problem.

Nanchang Rebuilds the Confucian Temple; Chairman Chiang Saved It Before; The Local Gentry of the Province Discuss Building It Later

Nanchang Correspondence: Since the Nanchang Confucian Temple was destroyed by wind and rain in the autumn of the 16th year of the Republic of China, it has been reduced to rubble. In the 17th year, former Chairman Zhu transformed the original site of the Confucian Temple into Dachen Park, which was presided over by former Mayor Wu. Later, due to the lack of a person in charge, it was repeatedly used by troops for stationing, grazing cattle, and raising horses, causing irreparable damage. The so-called park is only in name. At the beginning of Chairman Chiang's visit to Jiangxi, he believed that troops should not be stationed in the Confucian Temple and ordered the provincial government to repair it quickly and limited the time for the troops stationed there to move out. After receiving the order, the provincial government immediately sent workers to repair it day and night and had repaired the walls and inner railings. It was originally planned to restore the temple buildings, but the project was huge, and there was no funding, so it did not come to fruition. Therefore, flowers and trees were planted everywhere in the open space to temporarily preserve it. Now, provincial gentry Hu Siyi, Ouyang Wu, Wang Mingxuan, etc., believe that Jiangxi has suffered from banditry for six years, but it has not yet been eradicated. Heretical doctrines are rampant, and evildoers are rampant internally. The morals of the world and the hearts of the people have become extremely depraved. Those who are eager for quick success and instant benefits commit offenses against their superiors and cause chaos, changing their minds and contradicting themselves, without shame. All of this is because the rites and teachings are not clear, and the people have lost their central belief. Our country's cultural relics, rites, and righteousness have always revered Confucius. In recent years, the country has been in many troubles, and the Confucian temples in various places have been destroyed. There is no way to look up to them, so they should be rebuilt to worship Confucius, encourage the poor customs, and widely adopt good deeds. Banditry will be easily eradicated. They gathered all the gentry yesterday for discussion. Those present included Ouyang Wu, Hu Siyi, Fan Zhengbo, Peng Chengwan, Lu Fang, Cai Qian, He Zhihuan, Wang Shan, Wang Mingxuan, Li Shangyong, Zhong Youzu, and Xu Ruifu. It is heard that the decisions were: (1) First, those present were designated as promoters and contacted various members of the provincial government and the provincial party headquarters to join the promoters. (2) Xu Ruifu, Wang Mingxuan, and Lu Fang were selected to prepare and estimate the project. (3) Ouyang Jifu was selected to write the text. (Datong Society, October 26)

The Commotion in Guangzhou: Authorities Massively Arrest Dissidents; Bandits Throw Bombs in Protest; Japanese Arbitrarily Arrest People

Guangzhou Correspondence: Since Chen Jitang launched a massive search and arrest of dissidents, many have been implicated. Lian Bingzhang, the former division commander of the Fifth Army (Li Fulin's troops), has already been detained, and former subordinates of Lian who had no major involvement in the case have also been arrested. Zeng Feiwen, the former chief of staff of Li Fulin, is currently being held in the special room of the Provincial Public Security Bureau. In the navy, He Yilu, the captain of the Jiangda warship, was previously detained. Yesterday, Zhang Ruitong, the deputy captain of the Wufeng warship, was also arrested on suspicion. In the air force, a pilot surnamed Xu was arrested yesterday. Xu graduated from aviation school and has served in the aviation field for many years. The reason for his arrest is allegedly for plotting to mobilize the air force. In the Public Security Bureau, a law and regulations committee member surnamed Lan was detained yesterday on suspicion of being a reactionary. It is said that he has been interrogated and sentenced to death by firing squad. Because of this, a sense of terror has formed in official circles. Furthermore, in society, bandits have recently specialized in sending letters of extortion, placing bombs in prosperous markets and shops, causing unrest in the city. For example, various teahouses have been bombed by bandits more than once. On the evening of the 18th of this month, the Minsheng ferry, which travels between Xihao Estuary, Zhongshan, and Guangzhou, was also secretly bombed in the cabin by bandits. As passengers were gathering that night, a woman accidentally triggered the bomb, which exploded with a loud bang, injuring three female passengers on the ship: Ms. Xu Liang, Ms. Yang Ou, and Ms. Xie. By the time the water police arrived to investigate, the bandits had disappeared. As for diplomacy, Japan has recently adopted a proactive attitude towards Guangdong, first demanding protection for Japanese merchants and second demanding the disbandment of anti-Japanese groups in various places. Recently, it has become even more outrageous. On the 12th of this month, they arbitrarily arrested resident Koreans in Guangzhou. Initially, three Japanese and three Koreans took a car to Yang's residence in Zhuyuan Village, Gospel Village, Dongshan, on the 9th to inquire about the person named Jin Dousan. Jin happened to be out, so a friend, Park Uigil (also Korean), came out to deal with them, answering that Jin Dousan was not here. The Japanese then asked Park Uigil for his name, and Park truthfully told them. The Japanese then left. On the 12th, the three Japanese drove to Zhuyuan again and forcibly arrested Park Uigil and put him in the car without explanation, speeding away. As they passed Dongshan Road, Park Uigil shouted for help. Police heard the noise and wanted to step forward to inquire, but the car had already sped away. They only saw the license plate number as 612. Later, after checking the license plate, they learned that it was the car of the Japanese consulate, and that the arrested person was Park Uigil, a Korean living at Yang's residence in Zhuyuan. The owner of Yang's residence, Yang Shaobi, was originally Korean but has become a Chinese citizen. He has been living in Guangdong for two years, selling ginseng. Park is in the same business and came here two months ago, staying at his house. The authorities believe that the Japanese arbitrarily arresting residents within our territory is a grave violation of international law and have lodged a protest. After Park Uigil was arrested by the Japanese, he was detained in Shamian and temporarily placed in the custody of the French Concession consulate. Recently, the Japanese warship Sagami has been wired to sail into the provincial river, and it is possible that Park will be transferred elsewhere. When the warship sailed from the waters off Shantou, Japanese sailors once landed at Renshan Port in Huizhou, investigating the local household registration and the number of stationed troops, spying for a long time before leaving. The Guangdong government will also raise this point for negotiation. Due to the various disturbances in domestic and foreign affairs mentioned above, the authorities believe that strict precautions are necessary for public safety. They have convened a meeting and decided to hold winter defense exercises ahead of schedule, setting November 1st as the start date for the winter defense martial law period, with the Gendarmerie Headquarters and the Provincial Public Security Bureau responsible for the entire martial law. It is also planned to restore the joint military-police office, with personnel from the General Headquarters' Military Affairs Department, the Gendarmerie Headquarters, and the Provincial Public Security Bureau jointly organizing it. The winter defense martial law is being drafted. The Gendarmerie Headquarters has decided to form a bicycle patrol team of about a hundred people, who will patrol the city streets daily in shifts. All inspectors and detectives of the Public Security Bureau will patrol in shifts on the evening of the 1st, and additional security teams will be dispatched to key locations to check pedestrians' gun permits. Secret agents will be assigned to hotels and entertainment venues for careful inspection to ensure thoroughness and maintain public safety. (October 20th)

The Northern Route Army Defeats Zhu Mao at Zixi: Joint Air and Ground Bombardment; Killing Over Seven Thousand Bandits

Nanchang Correspondence: The Zhu Mao pseudo-First Front Army fiercely attacked Xiaoshi, Xunpu, Lichuan, Zuofang, and other places at the beginning of last month. Unable to succeed, they retreated into Fujian's border areas. From the 20th of this month, Zhu Mao again concentrated bandits in the Guangze area, launching a large-scale attack on the border areas. Their strategy was to use the pseudo-3rd Army Corps' Peng Dehuai's troops' pseudo-5th regiment's Dong Zhentang's division as the left flank, attacking the south of the Zixi Bridge from Lichuan, and the pseudo-1st Army Corps' Lin Biao's troops' pseudo-5th Army Corps' Dong Zhentang's other division as the right flank, attacking the north of the Zixi Bridge, attempting to cut off the traffic between Nancheng, Lichuan, Zixi, and Jinxi, and then divide and conquer a part of the National Revolutionary Army, hoping to seize supplies and weapons. At that time, the Wu Qiwai, Zhao Guantao, and Zhou Hunyuan's armies along the Xinfeng, Xiaoshi, Lichuan, and Zixi lines bravely resisted. The bandit masses came one after another, covering the mountains and fields. The National Revolutionary Army then dispatched bomber squadrons to assist in the battle, hovering over the bandit area, concentrating fire, and bombing the densely packed bandit formations, dropping many 50-kilogram bombs. On the 23rd, the battle was the fiercest, with the bandit masses suffering heavy casualties. Finally, they retreated along their original route. The headquarters and provincial government have just received a victory telegram from the front lines on the 24th, stating that over seven thousand bandits were killed in this battle. When the bandits collapsed and retreated, they were extremely disorganized, abandoning countless firearms and weapons. They are currently being pursued. (October 26th)

Bandits on the Hunan-Hubei Railway Intercept and Rob Trains: Several Passengers Killed and Injured by Stray Bullets; Chang'anling Station Robbed Clean

Hankou Correspondence: On the 18th of this month, when a train on the Hunan-Hubei Railway passed the Po Station, a freight car suddenly caught fire, burning four cars, resulting in significant losses. The Railway Bureau is strictly investigating to clarify the truth. Before ten days had passed, there was another incident of bandits robbing a train, injuring passengers with bullets, robbing the station, and destroying the tracks. This incident was even more serious than the previous one. The slow train heading north on the railway departed from Changsha to Hubei on the afternoon of the 26th. Rumors spread that the train was carrying over 100,000 yuan in cash, which aroused the bandits' covetousness. At 1:00 AM on the 27th, when the train passed the Chang'anling Station in Linxiang, dozens of bandits swarmed in, firing bullets like rain, and destroying the railway tracks and telegraph lines. They robbed the train. However, the section of the railway destroyed by the bandits was at the southern end of the train, so it could still travel north, allowing the train to escape quickly and reach Puqi Station, which was a safe area. Upon inspection of the train, although no property was lost, several passengers were injured by stray bullets, one of whom died from serious injuries. The driver was also injured. At noon that day, the train arrived at the Xujiapeng Station in Wuchang, delayed by four hours. The injured passengers were all sent to the hospital for treatment. The bandits, failing to rob the train, robbed the Chang'anling Station clean and left triumphantly. After the incident, the Hunan-Hubei Railway Bureau received a report and immediately sent workers to repair the tracks and telegraph lines that night. On the 28th, traffic resumed as usual. As for where the bandits escaped, it is not yet known. The 19th Division of Li Jue's troops stationed in Yuezhou and the 33rd Division of Feng Xingxian's troops stationed in Puqi have all dispatched teams to search and suppress them. (October 27th)

Financial Turmoil in Kaifeng: Tongheyu Bank Experiences a Run; Liu Zhi Strongly Urges Banks to Maintain Support

Kaifeng Correspondence: Recently, major banks in Kaifeng have adopted a non-cooperative attitude towards local private banks, leading to the collapse of Xinchang and a run on Tongheyu. The authorities, recognizing the significant impact on the city's finances, have been striving to maintain the support for all banks. Ten days ago, Liu Zhi instructed the director of the Construction Department to convene banks such as Central, China, Communications, Shanghai, and Jincheng to discuss measures to support Tongheyu. The provincial government also issued a notice limiting depositors to withdraw no more than 500 yuan for current accounts and prohibiting withdrawals for fixed-term accounts from the 14th to the 24th. In the past ten days, the public's sentiment has stabilized slightly. The major banks agreed to provide 560,000 yuan in support to Tongheyu for working capital. The banks initially aimed to bring down Tongheyu. Their willingness to offer support at the time was merely to appease the government and pretend to cooperate. Therefore, after the decision was made, the banks initially used the issue of collateral as an excuse to refuse support. Later, after Tongheyu's Xinxiang Electric Company and 700,000 yuan worth of coal in Jiaozuo, totaling over one million yuan, were pledged, they still refused to provide funds. During this negotiation period, only Henan Agricultural and Industrial Bank provided 50,000 yuan. The other banks only paid a few thousand yuan under the personal guarantee of Liu Zhi and the Chamber of Commerce. Therefore, the people of Kaifeng are quite dissatisfied with the banks.

Tongheyu depositors believe that the run on Tongheyu was purely caused by the exclusion of competitors. They recently organized a representative committee to discuss measures to support the bank. The committee held its first meeting the day before yesterday, resolving to automatically limit withdrawals and deciding on three measures to maintain Tongheyu's operations: (1) Request the government to extend the withdrawal measures announced on October 14th for ten days. (2) Request the government to use political influence to contact the banks and fulfill the previous agreement, raising 560,000 yuan within seven days to meet the demand for current account withdrawals. (3) The run on Tongheyu has caused panic in the market's finances. The government has repeatedly asked the banks to provide support, but the banks initially agreed and then changed their minds. The representative committee should warn the banks.

The provincial government's announcement limiting withdrawals expired on the 24th. Because the banks had not fully fulfilled the agreement to provide funds, the depositors' representative committee submitted a request to the provincial government to extend the measures for ten days, which was approved. Liu Zhi also sent telegrams to the head offices of Central, Communications, and other banks, urging them to support, stating, "To Mr. Kong Yongzhi, President of the Central Bank of Shanghai, Mr. Zhang, General Manager of the Bank of China, Mr. Tang, General Manager of the Bank of Communications, Mr. Chen, General Manager of the Bank of Shanghai, and Mr. Zhou, General Manager of the Jincheng Bank: I have learned that since the financial panic occurred in Kaifeng, Tongheyu Bank has also been affected by the run, and the situation is critical. I have previously telegraphed you, stating that the matter concerns the finances of the entire province, requesting your Bians office to provide support. In addition to pledging sufficient property, I am responsible for ensuring that your bank does not suffer any losses. Although your head office replied that it would provide support, after discussing with your office for many days, even maintaining a sum of 1,000 to 2,000 yuan per day has not been implemented, causing the people of Kaifeng to be very agitated towards your office. I am deeply afraid that accidents may occur and feel ashamed towards your bank. I propose that you find a way to remedy the situation, appease public anger, and avoid trouble. Please telegraph your instructions immediately. Respectfully, Liu Zhi" (October 25th)

Shanxi Coal Cannot Be Sold: Exorbitant Freight Rates Cause Factories to Close

Taiyuan Correspondence: China's coal industry is known to be rich. In recent years, foreign coal has been dumped in the market, and the situation has been worsening. Domestic coal factories have been greatly affected, with some suspending operations and others reducing their workforce. Since the September 18th Incident, coal shortages have occurred in various places, and the Shanxi coal industry has been particularly affected. An investigation revealed that the main reason is the excessively high freight rates, especially on the PingSui and ZhengTai railways. As a result, domestic coal cannot be sold smoothly, and foreign coal takes the opportunity to enter the market. Mining companies are closing down one after another, making it difficult to sustain operations. The details of coal transportation on various railways in North China are investigated and recorded below for the reference of those concerned about China's coal industry.

ZhengTai Railway

In terms of coal quality, the anthracite coal produced in Pingding, Shanxi, and the clean coal produced in Datong are both excellent. In terms of reserves, Shanxi's mines have more than 5.6 trillion tons, enough to supply the world for thousands of years, which has long been coveted by foreigners. However, due to the high freight rates, it is not possible to fully exploit and supply the needs of various places. The freight rates set by the ZhengTai Railway vary greatly for different mines. The lowest is for Jingxing coal, with a freight rate of 0.0062147 yuan per ton per kilometer. The next is for Baochang and Minxing coal, with a freight rate of 0.01810527 yuan per ton per kilometer. The next is for Zhengfeng coal, with a freight rate of 0.009412 yuan per ton per kilometer. The highest is for Yangquan Baojin coal, with a freight rate of 0.025 yuan per ton per kilometer, which is almost four times higher than that of Jingxing coal. The railway also has a rebate system, but the limits are too high, making it difficult to enjoy in practice. For example, for Class A rebates, from 10,001 tons to 20,000 tons, the rebate is only 4.4 yuan per car (25 tons or less), with a freight rate of 0.0235868 yuan per ton per kilometer. From 20,001 tons to 40,000 tons, the rebate is 5 yuan per car, with a freight rate of 0.0233885 yuan per ton per kilometer. From 40,001 tons to 60,000 tons, the rebate is 5.6 yuan per car, with a freight rate of 0.0231908 yuan per ton per kilometer. For more than 60,000 tons, the rebate is 6.25 yuan per car, with a freight rate of 0.0229753 yuan per ton per kilometer. The Class B rebate system is divided into four categories: 60,000 tons to 120,000 tons, 120,000 tons to 180,000 tons, 180,000 tons to 240,000 tons, and more than 240,000 tons. The amount of rebate is determined by the amount of tonnage. On the surface, it seems to be preferential, but in reality, Yangquan anthracite coal cannot be transported out of more than 60,000 tons per month due to the railway's small cars and narrow tracks, and there is no hope of this. Therefore, the Class B rebate system is equivalent to drawing a cake to satisfy hunger. This is the main reason why Shanxi coal cannot be exported.

PingHan Railway

The PingHan coal transportation is lower than ZhengTai. The treatment is also inconsistent. For example, the freight rate for each ton and kilometer of coal from the Liuhegou, Fuzhong, Yili, and Zhengfeng mines is 0.006825 yuan, while the freight rate for Jingjing coal is 0.011935 yuan per ton and kilometer (calculated at 70% of the ordinary freight rate of the PingHan railway). The freight rate for Shanxi coal is 0.01705 yuan per ton and kilometer (calculated according to item 32 of the ordinary freight rate of the PingHan railway). Not only can Shanxi coal not enjoy the same preferential treatment of 0.006825 yuan as Liuhegou Fuzhong Yili, but it cannot be given the same reduced rate of 70% as Jingjing coal.

PingSui Railway

The PingSui Railway previously had a special export price for coal from northern Shanxi, which was about 0.01662 yuan. Later, it was heard that the mine owners requested a reduction, and it was changed to 0.0091811 yuan. However, it is still limited to one year, and only those who export can enjoy this special price.

BeiNing Railway

The freight rate for coal on this railway is 0.008004 yuan and 0.00734 yuan per ton per kilometer for Kailuan coal, and 0.006667 yuan per ton per kilometer for Beipiao coal. For other coal mines, the special price for export from Fengtai to Tanggu is 0.01 yuan per ton per kilometer, and the ordinary freight rate is calculated at 80%, which is 0.01359 yuan per ton per kilometer.

Other Railways

In addition, the freight rate for Hanyeping on the Hunan-Hubei Railway is 0.00642 yuan per ton per kilometer, and the freight rate for Luda coal on the Jiaoji Railway is 0.00761 yuan per ton per kilometer. The freight rate for each coal from Chinese-owned coal mines is 0.0072 yuan. Therefore, although China's coal reserves are rich, the current output is very small. Of the annual consumption of 25 to 26 million tons, domestic coal only accounts for 11 million tons, which is less than half. The rest is dumped by foreign coal. The main reason is the high freight rates, which make the cost very high and cannot be sold throughout the country. Among them, Shanxi's coal reserves are the richest, and the freight rates of the ZhengTai and PingSui railways are the highest, resulting in coal produced in Yangquan and Datong being piled up like mountains and unable to be sold (it is heard that coal factories in the Datong area can produce 5,000 tons of coal per day). Currently, due to the excessively high coal transportation costs on the PingSui Railway, production has been reduced due to its inability to sell. Only 300 to 400 tons are produced per day. Coal factories are forced to lay off workers and reduce their scale, allowing goods to be abandoned on the ground and increasing unemployment. It is truly lamentable. If efforts are not made to remedy the situation urgently, the future is dangerous and unimaginable. (October 24th)

Songjiang's First District Plans to Establish Experimental Townships

The various townships under the jurisdiction of the First District Office of this county are handling local self-government quite diligently. District Head Zhong believes that the First District is located in the urban and suburban areas, with convenient transportation by road and rail. People from various institutions often come to Songjiang to inspect municipal administration and local self-government. In order to promote local self-government and improve municipal construction, the district plans to imitate the experimental township methods of the various districts of Qingpu County, and first designate one or two towns in each district as experimental towns. The township offices will actively carry out matters that they should handle to observe the actual effects. This was brought up for discussion at the district affairs meeting on the 28th, and was passed in principle. However, the method for raising funds for the experimental towns will be determined after inquiring about Qingpu County's methods.

Private Salt Smugglers Arrested for Resisting Arrest

Yang Zilong, a resident of Punan, is a well-known salt smuggler. Recently, he smuggled a large batch of private salt, planning to transport it to the Xia'ang Bridge area for sale. When the ship passed by the Tuolai Temple, it was spotted by a police officer from the eighth district of the tax police, who ordered it to stop for inspection. Yang and another salt smuggler, Pan Zhuangzi, resisted arrest. The police arrested Yang and others and took them to the district for preliminary interrogation. As the case involved private salt, the police were dispatched to the county court prosecutor's office yesterday morning for interrogation. The two defendants were ordered to be detained pending review.

Suzhou's Wanniang Bridge Fundraises for Reconstruction

Wanniang Bridge, outside of Xumen, is the largest bridge in Suzhou and an important transportation route for both water and land traffic outside Xumen. However, the stone steps on both sides are very high, making it difficult for vehicles to pass. Now, local business leaders such as Ji Xiaosong have initiated the reconstruction of the bridge with reinforced concrete, which will cost about 10,490 yuan in labor and materials. Yesterday (28th), County Magistrate Zou convened local people to discuss fundraising methods. It was decided to submit a request to the Construction Department for funding.

District Head Embezzles Funds and Is Dismissed for Investigation

Sun Zheng, the district head of the Fifteenth District, embezzled wages for digging trenches during the Shanghai War. After being reported to the county government by Zou Gu, the head of the township, and others, County Magistrate Zou summoned Sun for questioning on the 27th. Believing that there was indeed a major suspicion, he issued a hand-written order yesterday (28th) to dismiss the district head first and await investigation. Pan Bangjun, the district head of the Sixth District, was temporarily appointed to fill the vacancy. Qin Zhonghuai was dispatched to the township for detailed investigation and reporting for review.

Wuxi Loan Collection Fails and Ends in Hanging Suicide

Xi Huian, the owner of Huisheng Silk Factory under Huigong Bridge in this county, was affected by the sharp decline in the silk market and owed more than 30,000 yuan. He took his family and fled to Shanghai on the 17th of this month. He also sent a letter to the county chamber of commerce, asking it to clear the factory's debt. After receiving the letter, the chamber of commerce considered it difficult to clear the debt based on Xi Huian's empty words. It immediately forwarded the letter to the silk factory industry association, advising Xi to return to Wuxi and discuss with the creditors in good faith to find a proper solution. However, Xi never returned. The creditors were all worried about this situation. Qin Gengmo, a resident of Zhangjing Bridge in the Seventh District, was also one of the creditors. The portion of the debt owed by Huisheng Factory was 3,250 yuan. This sum was collected by Qin from 284 silkworm farmers. Now, the farmers are demanding repayment from Qin, who is unable to pay. Disputes have arisen. The day before yesterday, Qin's wife, Wu, came to the city and sat at Xi's house in Dunrenli to demand repayment, but she did not receive a single penny. Suddenly, she had the thought of committing suicide, and she went upstairs and hanged herself. Later, she was discovered by Xi's mother-in-law, Zhu, who managed to save her. It was fortunate that it did not lead to a life-threatening incident. More than ten people, including Zou Housheng, the owner of Gongchang Cocoon Company, were also forced by the farmers to sit at Xi's house to demand repayment. They jointly sent a letter to the county chamber of commerce, asking it to uphold justice and provide relief. The factory has more than 2,000 packages of dried cocoons stored in Yixin Storehouse, more than 50 loads of silk, 300+ packages of Hixiecheng cocoons, and 500+ packages of Ruichang cocoons that had been loaned to banks such as Jiangsu Bank. After receiving the letter, the chamber of commerce sent staff member Ji Songzhen to contact the relevant cocoon stores and banks. It also sent a letter to the silk and cocoon industry associations, requesting them to urge Xi Huian to return to Wuxi as soon as possible and clear the debts with all parties in order to maintain the credit of the silk and cocoon industry and avoid disputes.

Two Arrested in the Dazhuxiang Murder Case

Zhang Renjin, a resident of Houtangqiao Township, 66th Tu, Second District (Jingyun City), who worked as a bowl repairer, went out to repair bowls on the 11th of this month. When he passed through Dazhuxiang, 595 Tu in the same district, he was suddenly beaten to death by Zhu Quangen, Zhu Xianghe, Zhu Du, Lu A'tu, and others. They moved the body to the railway tracks next to 596 Tu. After examination by the map head, it was confirmed that the death was caused by injuries. However, the perpetrators were still at large. After a thorough investigation by Prosecutor Shen Zhaoming, who was in charge of the case, he issued several arrest warrants the day before yesterday, ordering law enforcement officials Fang Peisheng, Feng Yongbao, Zhou Yizhu, Jiang Yuanzhu, and others to go to the countryside to arrest the perpetrators. Zhu Xianghe and Zhu Du were arrested on the spot. The others are still at large. The two perpetrators were escorted to the court, and after interrogation by Prosecutor Shen, they were ordered to be detained pending the arrest of the remaining perpetrators before further legal action is taken.

County Court Burns Opium

After confiscating opium and opium paraphernalia found in investigations within the county, the county court of this county has consistently made a policy to publicly burn the drugs, as a symbol of cleaning up drug. From April to the end of September this year, a total of 171 pieces of evidence confiscated from opium cases were burned on the 28th of this month. Prior to the burning, Chief Judge Xu and Chief Zhou submitted a request to the High Court to send personnel to supervise the burning, and they also sent letters to various agencies and organizations to attend the burning. At 1:00 PM yesterday, the burning was scheduled. The High Court sent Secretary Zhang to Wuxi to supervise the destruction. Chief Judge Xu and Chief Zhou ordered the bailiffs to move the drugs to the courtyard and set them on fire. Many people came to watch the burning, and they all praised the action.

Zhenjiang's Hong Fuyuan's Request for Bail Denied

Hong Fuyuan, the former magistrate of Pixian County, was detained by the provincial government for alleged corruption for more than a year. After Chairman Chen came to the province, he ordered all corrupt criminals to be transferred to the court for trial. Now, Hong Fuyuan's son, Hong Xiyi, has filed a petition with the court, requesting bail for his father. After reviewing the arguments, the procurator general stated that Hong's case was serious and that bail was not appropriate under the law. Yesterday, an instruction was issued, stating, "The petition has been noted. Your father's case is a major dereliction of duty case transferred by the provincial government, and it is currently under strict investigation. The request is difficult to approve."

Suspension of Licenses of Pulled Rickshaws

The Zhenjiang County Government previously received instructions from the Construction Department regarding a case in which merchants had petitioned for the licensing of pulled rickshaws for commercial operation. The county government was instructed to investigate, verify, and deliberate on the matter. It was submitted to the seventh political affairs meeting of the county for discussion. It was agreed that there are currently 850 pulled rickshaws in operation, and 100 rickshaws are privately owned by the rickshaw pullers, which is already more than enough. The licenses of old rickshaw companies that were previously revoked, and for which the county was ordered to allow their resumption when there were sufficient vehicles, have not yet been restored. Before the roads in the provincial capital are fully completed, it seems that there is no need to license more pulled rickshaws. It was decided to temporarily suspend the licensing of new pulled rickshaws. The county government submitted the resolution to the Construction Department for review. After reviewing the report, the Construction Department instructed the county government yesterday to approve the temporary suspension of licenses.

Yangzhou Youth Castrates Himself in Religious Fervor

Xu Zhilin, age twenty-three, residing at No. 18 Yujing Street in this city, was extremely filial to his parents. He had two older brothers, both of whom were married and established. Zhilin was an apprentice at Zhang Litai's cartwright shop in Guqiting but later became idle at home. He was a devout Buddhist, chanting "Amitabha" daily. Yesterday (the 26th) at 8 PM, Zhilin burned incense and prostrated himself, chanting Buddhist scriptures. He then went to the backyard, grabbed a sharp axe, and ran out with blood streaming from his hands. He rushed out the door, and his family chased after him, but he disappeared. He was intercepted by police officer Yang Hui near Beidajie. Zhilin threw the axe and his severed testicles on the ground. He was sent to Dasheng Hospital on Zuo Wei Street, where Director Jiang bandaged him. The police officer then took Zhilin home. It was reported that he had briefly lost consciousness but then revived. His mother wept upon seeing him. While in a coma from the severe injury, Zhilin continued to chant "Amitabha," comforting his mother with words like, "I'll be fine, I'll be reborn, and you'll all benefit." The superstition of the ignorant is both laughable and pitiful.

Clerk Dismissed for Forging Documents

Fang Mianzhi had previously served as a clerk in the Jiangdu County office. He was later sentenced to ten months in prison for bribery. After serving his term, he was unemployed for a long time and his livelihood was very difficult. He wanted to return to his position as a clerk. When Magistrate Ma took office, he was very strict about the collection of grain and money from the various departments and believed that there were many abuses. Fang took advantage of this opportunity to repeatedly forge letters of introduction from authorities in Beijing and the provinces. Magistrate Ma ignored the letters because the wording did not sound like his own. Fang continued to pester him, so Magistrate Ma summoned him to the office to inquire about the origin of the letters and his relationship with the senders. Fang claimed they were from relatives and friends, but he had secretly inquired and was denied by all parties. The police were ordered to detain Fang and send him to court for punishment. The forged letters were from Zhou Renru, secretary of a district regiment, Pan Yunzhai and Ye Xiufeng of the Central Party Headquarters, and Zhao Dihua, director of the Finance Department.

Sima Town Adds Postal Money Order Services

Sima Town in the fifth district of this county is located on the banks of the Yangtze River and is an important transportation hub with thriving businesses. However, it lacks financial institutions for remittances. It has been reported that the town's postal agency has been approved by the postal authorities to add postal money order services to facilitate remittances for merchants and residents. The limit is reportedly ten yuan, and the service began the day before yesterday.

Bandit Hu Xiaoxiong Executed in Nanhui

Hu Xiaoxiong, a notorious bandit from Nicheng in the fifth district, colluded with others in May of last year to rob several residents, including Mao Quanfa, Liu Yulin, and Tang Jinfa. He poured kerosene on Mao Quanfa's wife, causing fatal burns. The victims reported the crime to the county government, which ordered the police to apprehend the suspect in Shanghai and bring him back to the county. Under interrogation, he confessed to colluding with Lao Longban, Chen Xinglin, Liu Genfa, Mao Muxiang, Chen Xingshan, Gu Shengxiang, and others, who were still at large, to repeatedly rob the homes of Mao Quanfa and others. The county government proposed a death sentence, which was approved by the Jiangsu Provincial Government. Yesterday morning at 9 AM, the county government brought the convict Hu Xiaoxiong to the execution grounds outside the South Gate, verified his identity, and executed him by firing squad.

Jiangyin Holds Exhibition of National Products

The county Party headquarters, under orders, held a National Products Movement propaganda week and a National Products Exhibition. The executive committee decided to organize propaganda teams from various agencies and schools to spread the message. Today (the 27th), the National Products Exhibition was held at the People's Education Center, displaying cotton yarn from local yarn factories, Hua Cheng Yonghua double-sided paper, Ziyou cloth, Tianlun Vienna cloth, flannel, and products from thirty to forty other factories. Many people from all walks of life came to visit.

Quarrel Between Husband and Wife Leads to Murder

Yang Fusheng, a farmer from Zhangjiadai in Qiren Township, Shazhou, and his adopted son, Yang Genpei, had an argument on the 22nd of this month. His wife, Lin Di, was pushed and killed by her husband. The third district chief, Zhu Wen, reported the incident to the county. On the 26th, investigator Shi Cheng and a coroner were sent to the village to conduct an autopsy. The deceased was three months pregnant, and a violent fall caused bleeding from her mouth, nose, and lower body, resulting in internal injuries and death. The suspect, Yang Genpei, was taken to the county for interrogation on the 27th.

Salt Prices Increase in Five Districts of Jiangsu

The Ministry of Finance's plan to reorganize the national salt tax has been approved. The reorganized tax rates for the five districts of Jiangsu are as follows: (1) Baoshan, Jiading, Taicang, Kunshan, Qingpu, Songjiang, Fengxian, Jinshan, Zhenjiang, Danyang, Wujin, Jiangyin, Jingjiang, Jintan, Liyang, Yixing, and Jianping districts will increase from 6.7 yuan to 7.1 yuan, an increase of 0.4 yuan. (2) Baoshan Jieyi Jiushang Nanchuansha, Shanghai Concession will increase from 4.5 yuan to 5.5 yuan, an increase of 1 yuan. (3) Chongqi will increase from 3 yuan to 4 yuan, an increase of 1 yuan. (4) Hengsha and other districts will increase from 0.6 yuan to 1 yuan, an increase of 0.4 yuan. The new rates will take effect on October 22nd of this year, as ordered by the Ministry of Finance to the Salt Affairs Audit Office, which instructed the Songjiang Salt Transport Vice Commissioner to order the salt merchant guilds of the five districts of Jiangsu to comply.

Zhang Xiaoruo Reorganizes Industries in Nantong

Zhang Xiaoruo, a native of this county, has been stationed in Shanghai in recent years due to his yarn factory and shipping business. He returned to Nantong on the 27th for a stay of about a month to begin reorganizing local industries. The flour mill and iron factory will start operations within the month. Preparations are being made to raise capital for Dasheng No. 2 Factory, which will also resume operations in the short term. The Tianshenggang Power Plant is making active progress and will be able to generate electricity by next spring. The coastal dike for land reclamation and animal husbandry was previously breached by the tide and will be inspected and repaired.

Suppressing Salt Smugglers in Baochang

A large group of salt smugglers in Baochang, eastern county, is resisting tax police and have shot and injured the police chief. They are acting very brazenly. Tax police chief Xu Yonghua of the fourth district is leading a team, together with county police, to suppress them.

Robbery at Dongwang Temple Town in Liuhe

Dongwang Temple Town in the eighth district of this county, located near the border of Jiangsu and Anhui provinces, was suddenly attacked at around 10 PM the day before yesterday by more than twenty bandits speaking with Anhui accents. They carried firearms and other weapons and broke into Wu Gongxing's cloth store. Store owners Wu Mingzheng and Wu Mingshan, seeing the bandits' ferocity, used a quick-firing gun from their home to resist. However, they were outnumbered, and Wu took the opportunity to escape. The bandits seized the opportunity to search the store, resulting in a loss of about six to seven hundred yuan.

Jiashan Lawyer Shi Naixiu Seeks Divorce from His Wife

Shi Naixiu (also known as Shi Feixian), a native of this county who practices law in Shanghai, married Yang Xiuying (i.e., Yang Yingqiu), a female educator who lived nearby, ten years ago after falling in love. At that time, their love was very strong, and they had a son named Yunguan. Shi was hired as a tutor by Yao Xinji's business in Shanghai. During the Qi-Lu War, Shi took Yang to Shanghai and, through a friend's introduction, took on educational duties at several girls' schools. Before long, Shi became involved with someone else and abandoned Yang. Yang returned to Bixian to earn a living on her own. After several years, Shi, with Yang still present, was unable to marry his new love openly. He offered several thousand dollars to persuade Yang to remarry, but Yang remained steadfast. She filed a lawsuit in the local court, which remained unresolved for a long time. In 1930, Shi accused Yang of seriously insulting him and sued Yang in the High Court, appealing to the Supreme Court, which found the appeal to be without merit and dismissed the original lawsuit. It has now been learned that Shi has filed a criminal lawsuit against Yang in the Shanghai District Court, while Yang has hired lawyer Zhu Taiqing to sue Shi in civil court and is seeking the unanimous support of local women's associations. The sensational Shi-Yang divorce case is of wide interest, but how it will be resolved remains to be seen.

Local News

Finance Minister Song's Resignation is Firm, Kong Xiangxi Summoned to Beijing Yesterday; Li Shizeng Entrusted by Wang to Urge Song to Return to His Post; New Developments Expected After Chairman Chiang Returns to Beijing; Mayor Wu Says Premier Wang Will Come to Retain Him

While various parties are still earnestly trying to retain Finance Minister Song Ziwen, Mr. Song did not go to his office at the Ministry of Finance yesterday and remained secluded. Chairman Chiang also returned to Nanjing by plane from Jiangxi yesterday afternoon. As a result of mediation by various parties, a considerable decision seems to have been reached. Kong Xiangxi, Governor of the Central Bank, was summoned to Beijing yesterday afternoon at 4 PM to discuss financial measures. Details of the situation are reported below.

Summary of Mr. Song's Resignation

Rumors of Minister Song's resignation have been rampant recently. Yesterday, reporters repeatedly inquired at the Ministry of Finance office and confirmed the news. They also learned the contents of the resignation from other sources. It stated that since the January 28th Incident, he had shouldered the heavy responsibility of finance, maintaining it with difficulty, and that he was physically and mentally exhausted, fearing that he would mismanage the country's major affairs. He requested to resign from all his positions. It is also heard that Minister Song's intention to resign is extremely firm, and despite various attempts to retain him, he has shown no signs of withdrawing his resignation.

Still Not Working, No Longer Denying

After Mr. Song's resignation was confirmed, it was no longer denied. Yesterday morning at 10 AM, reporters from various newspapers went to the Ministry of Finance office to see Mr. Song and submitted written inquiries asking: (1) Is the resignation true? (2) In addition to the position of Minister of Finance, will he also resign from his concurrent positions as Vice President of the Executive Yuan and Standing Committee Member of the Economic Committee? (3) Request to publish the original text of the resignation. As a result, Mr. Song, claiming to be busy, still sent Councilor Qin Yingchun to answer on his behalf, formally acknowledging that Minister Song had submitted his resignation to the Central Government and that the resignation letter had been sent to the Central Government on the 25th. He resigned primarily as Minister of Finance, and everything else would be left to the Central Government. Yesterday, Mr. Song rested at home, did not go to the Ministry of Finance office, and declined all visitors. Only Chen Xing and others visited him in the morning, and he did not personally meet with other important figures who came to visit.

Key Finance Officials to Continue Their Responsibilities

Mr. Song has been meeting with Zou Lin, the Vice Minister of Finance, Li Tiaosheng, the Administrative Vice Minister, various directors-general, and other key officials at his residence for several days. It is said they are discussing the handover of duties. However, key finance officials are determined to continue their responsibilities. According to Mr. Qin Yingchun, a councilor at the Ministry of Finance, Minister Song's resignation is a personal matter, and the staff of the Ministry of Finance will not resign or advance simultaneously. Because the key finance officials are appointed by the government, they must continue their responsibilities and will not advance or retreat based on Minister Song's departure.

Various Parties Mediating and Earnestly Trying to Retain

After Minister Song's resignation was sent to Nanjing, President Wang cabled Chairman Chiang and entrusted Li Shizeng to come to Shanghai to persuade Mr. Song to withdraw his resignation. Mr. Li arrived in Shanghai on the 26th and went directly to see Mr. Song after getting off the train. They talked for about two hours before he left. He visited again the next day, earnestly urging Mr. Song to return to his post. Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng also visited Mr. Song the day before yesterday, also to persuade him to withdraw his resignation. Chairman Chiang personally sent his wife to Shanghai to retain him the day after Mr. Song's resignation. Various parties in Nanjing also sent cables to both Jiangxi and Shanghai to mediate. Yesterday afternoon, Chairman Chiang flew back to Nanjing and, after detailed discussions with various parties, a considerable decision has been reached. The Central Government will handle the matter based on this opinion.

Kong Xiangxi Flew to Beijing Yesterday

Central Bank Governor Kong Xiangxi flew to Beijing yesterday afternoon at 4 PM on the Ford aircraft that flew from Nanjing to Shanghai at 1 PM yesterday. This was to discuss persuading Mr. Song to withdraw his resignation and financial measures with the Central Government. Mr. Kong's trip is, in fact, to mediate the stalemate.

Mayor Wu Says President Wang Will Come to Shanghai

Mr. Song went out to visit friends yesterday afternoon around 3:30 PM and did not return home until the evening. According to Mayor Wu, who visited Mr. Song the day before, he visited Mr. Song yesterday (i.e., the day before yesterday) in a personal capacity to urge him to withdraw his resignation. The Central Government will not allow Mr. Song to retire. President Wang will also come to Shanghai to meet with Mr. Song and retain him. It is hoped that Mr. Song will withdraw his resignation.

Shanghai Telegraph Office Implements Telephone Telegraph Service to Avoid Delivery Delays

According to Mr. Hua, the business manager of the Shanghai Telegraph Office, over one hundred merchants from Dalian and Shandong, as well as some foreign merchants, have a special agreement with the office to send and receive telegrams by telephone. Telegrams from Dalian, Tianjin, Beiping, Qingdao, Yantai, and other places are first reported to the recipient by telephone, and then the original telegram is delivered. If the sender also sends and receives telegrams by telephone, a reply can be received from Tianjin, Qingdao, and other places within ten minutes. Mr. Hua also stated that the telegraph office considers the above speed to be too slow. After the Creed high-speed telegraph machine is fully installed, the time required can be further reduced.

Huang Yunsou, the Chinese envoy to Mexico, after receiving orders, came to Shanghai a few days ago. Mr. Huang boarded the ship around 11 PM the night before, and his relatives and friends went to see him off. Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Responds to Wuxian Chamber of Commerce on Measures to Stop Dumping of Japanese Rice; Urges Government to Implement Dumping Tax; Restrains Merchants from Violating Agreements

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce previously received a cable from the Wuxian Chamber of Commerce requesting measures to prevent the dumping of Japanese rice in Shanghai and to maintain the price of domestic rice. It is now known that the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce has purchased a method and replied to the association. The letters and telegrams are recorded separately below.

Telegram from Wuxian

To the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce: Reports indicate that Japanese rice is being shipped to Shanghai for dumping, which hinders our country's agricultural production. At a time when the rural economy is declining, allowing the devaluation and sale of rice will inevitably depress the price of domestic rice. This will not only cause a loss of profits and economic panic, but also lead to the abandonment of agriculture and national unrest. Our association is concerned and cannot remain silent. We earnestly request you to take effective measures to prevent this in order to protect agriculture and save people's lives. We are very anxious. The Wuxian County Chamber of Commerce respectfully sends its greetings.

Reply from the Chamber of Commerce

To the Wuxian County Chamber of Commerce: On the 27th of this month, we received a telegram stating that Japanese rice is being shipped to Shanghai for dumping, requesting us to take measures to prevent this. We have found that for goods shipped to China from various countries, except for those prohibited by treaty agreements, we cannot unilaterally prohibit their import. Therefore, in terms of the government, the only way is to adopt a policy of prohibiting through taxation and to promptly implement import taxes on foreign rice. Although our association has repeatedly cabled to urge this, the government is still hesitant. We ask your association to follow this directive and urge this together. As for the merchants, the only way is to strictly restrain themselves from violating agreements. Shenfeng and other eight rice merchants, fearing public censure, are already applying to terminate their contracts. However, rice is not the only Japanese product being dumped in China, and since the end of the war on the Great Wall, solidarity has been noticeably weakening everywhere. We especially hope that your association will work hard to uplift this and prevent others from taking advantage. This is for the Wuxian County Chamber of Commerce.

Garrison Headquarters Convening Winter Defense Conference, November 4th, 1 PM

Shanghai Mayor and Songhu Garrison Commander Wu Tiecheng believes that with the arrival of winter, it is inevitable that bandits will hide and petty thieves will be active. To prevent this in advance and seek local peace, he has scheduled a winter defense conference at the Garrison Headquarters on November 4th at 1 PM to discuss methods for arresting bandits and ensuring the safety of the people. Li Xiehe Talks About National Destiny, Worrying About the Future; Social Economy Nearing Bankruptcy; Youth Frustrated and Feeling Hopeless

Datong News Agency reports that Central Committee member Li Liejun has been feeling unwell recently and is resting at his residence in Shanghai. A reporter from Datong News Agency visited Mr. Li at his private residence on Avenue Massenet yesterday and was granted an audience. Mr. Li did not discuss politics, but was very concerned about the economic panic of society. He said that in recent years, China's social economy has been collapsing. On the one hand, this is the result of the economic aggression of imperialists, but frequent natural and man-made disasters in the country have also contributed to it. The rural areas of the central provinces are already bankrupt, and only the provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang are relatively stable. In the past two years, due to the impact of the sharp drop in rice prices, rural society is also gradually facing bankruptcy. Shanghai is the essence of the whole country, but since the January 28th Incident, the social economy has also fallen into extreme panic. From what I know, shops on Nanjing Road have always been difficult to rent. Shops often spent huge sums of money to compete for business, but recently there have been many vacant shops, and no one cares about them. This proves the decline of various industries. The industrial and commercial industries are gradually showing signs of collapse. Shanghai is like this, and the interior is even worse. The number of unemployed people today is unknown. A large number of young people feel that there is no way out, and the near future is very worrying. Mr. Li also said that the current international situation is becoming increasingly dangerous, and the situation is becoming more and more difficult. If an international incident occurs, the future will be even more unimaginable.

National Railway Through Transportation Begins, Shanghai-Beiping Direct Freight Car Implemented Yesterday; One Round Trip Between Shanghai and Beiping Every Day; 402 Drove to Beiping Yesterday, 401 Drove to Shanghai Yesterday

The national railway is responsible for the joint transportation of goods, scheduled to be implemented on November 1. The Shanghai-Beiping direct joint transport freight car was implemented yesterday. There is one round trip between Shanghai and Beiping every day. The fourth zero one and fourth zero two are designated as the through trains for Shanghai-Beiping joint transport goods. The details are as follows.

Responsible Joint Transportation Scheduled for Implementation

The Ministry of Railways ordered the Beijing-Shanghai, Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo, Jinpu, Beining, Jiaoji, Longhai, PingSui, Zhengben, Daoqing, and XiangE railway bureaus to prepare for the national railway responsible for the joint transportation of goods. It promulgated the 42 articles of the Provisional Measures for the National Railway Responsible for the Joint Transportation of Goods. At the same time, it ordered the various railway bureaus to follow the ministry's current Freight Car Transportation Regulations, the current Freight Car Responsible Transportation Regulations, and the detailed rules for handling procedures, bills of lading procedures, and detailed rules for handling procedures. It was scheduled to be implemented on November 1. After implementation, if there is any loss of goods in responsible joint transportation during the responsible transportation period, the railway where the loss occurred will be responsible for compensation. If it cannot be proven on which railway the loss occurred, the railways that have transported the goods will share the compensation in proportion to the agreed transportation fee. The various railway bureaus have designated freight cars and are prepared. The various transfer stations have been determined, and the driving schedule has also been arranged.

Shanghai-Beiping Direct Freight Car Begins

The Beijing-Shanghai, Jinpu, and Beining Railway Bureaus were ordered by the Ministry to open the Shanghai-Beiping freight car, which was implemented on September 1. Due to a decrease in cargo, it was temporarily suspended until the 15th. The Capital Railway Ferry was opened on the 22nd of this month. The Ministry of Railways telegraphed the Beijing-Shanghai, Jinpu, and Beining Railways on the 28th of this month to first implement the Shanghai-Beiping direct joint transport freight car in preparation for the national railway to be responsible for the joint transportation of goods. After receiving the order, the three railway bureaus began to implement it yesterday. There is one round trip between Shanghai and Beiping every day. The fourth zero one and fourth zero two are designated as the Shanghai-Beiping direct joint transport freight cars. Yesterday, the fourth zero two departed from Shanghai Maigen Road Station at 5:20 PM, arrived at the Nanjing riverside at 6:40 AM this morning, and took the ferry across the river. It departed from Pukou at 3:20 PM and arrived in Tianjin at 11:45 AM tomorrow morning. It departed from Tianjin on the Beining Railway at 6:30 PM and arrived at Qianmen, Beiping, at 12:12 AM the day after tomorrow. Yesterday, the fourth zero one departed from Qianmen, Beiping, at 10:36 PM, arrived in Tianjin at 2:26 PM, and departed from Tianjin on the Jinpu Railway at 9 PM. It arrived in Pukou at 5:25 AM tomorrow morning, took the ferry, and departed from the Nanjing riverside at 2 PM, arriving at Shanghai Maigen Road Station at 6 AM the day after tomorrow.

Dr. Feng Zefang's Thoughts After Inspecting Cotton Production in Hubei

The Cotton Control Committee of the National Economic Council previously dispatched Mr. Sun Enchen and Mr. Feng Zefang to inspect cotton production in various provinces. Now, we record Dr. Feng's thoughts on the inspection of cotton production in Hubei, as follows: I (Mr. Feng referring to himself) arrived in Hankou on the 11th. On the morning of the 12th, I paid respects to the provincial authorities. In the afternoon, I began the inspection with Mr. Yang Xiandong, the chief technician of the Hubei Cotton Improvement Committee. On the same day, I visited the Committee's cotton seed farm in Luojia Mountain. On the 13th, I visited the Xujiapeng Experimental Farm and the Wufengdi Cotton Seed Farm. From the 14th to the 15th, I went to eastern Hubei for inspection, passing through Huangpi, Huanggang, Macheng, and other counties. From the 16th to the 20th, I inspected the Han River basin, passing through Hanyang, Hanchuan, Yunmeng, Yingcheng, Jingmen, Qianjiang, Tianmen, Mianyang, and other counties. Based on my observations, eastern Hubei is almost entirely planted with Chinese cotton. From Lijiaji to Macheng, the Chinese cotton I saw along the way had many bolls, proving its abundant yield. Moreover, in mid-October, the cotton bolls and fibers were almost entirely mature, indicating its early maturity, which is suitable for the need for two crops a year. However, the Chinese cotton seen in this area has fibers that are too coarse and short, mostly less than three-quarters of an inch, which is not suitable for spinning. It is advisable to promote the already improved Chinese cotton in this area, so that its fibers are longer than seven-eighths of an inch to one inch, to meet the needs of the yarn mills, while maintaining its original high yield and early maturity, etc., to suit the local agricultural conditions. As for whether American cotton can be planted in this area in the future, it still needs to be tested in the future. As for the Han River basin, the soil along the banks of the river from Shayang to Hankou is excellent alluvial soil, which is most suitable for cotton production and is truly a naturally suitable area for cotton. Along the way, from Shayang to Zhangjiegang, I saw mostly American cotton, and it was almost impossible to see traces of Chinese cotton. From Yuekou downwards, Chinese cotton fields and American cotton fields are mixed together, and in one field, Chinese cotton and American cotton are often mixed together. According to preliminary field investigations, the American cotton has mostly degenerated. The American cotton bolls are very small, the seeds are green and small, and the fibers are mostly shorter than seven-eighths of an inch. It matures late, and even on the 20th, when the plants are about to be pulled out, there are still many green bolls on the cotton plants that have not opened. Its yield cannot be estimated because farmers pick the cotton together with the boll husks when picking the cotton. According to farmers, the yield of American cotton is better than that of Chinese cotton, so the area planted with American cotton is increasing year by year. Based on this situation, in the Han River basin, where farmers are already accustomed to planting American cotton, it seems advisable to promote American cotton. Special attention should be paid to early-maturing varieties, because in the American cotton area, farmers still practice the two-crop-a-year system. The above is an emergency promotion method. As for which varieties should be promoted in Hubei Province in the future, there is no experimental basis at present, so it cannot be established. However, according to this preliminary observation, American cotton should pay attention to early maturity. 'Shuo Zi' cotton is the earliest maturing American cotton currently available in China, and it is very likely to be promoted. According to the results of the cooperative cotton planting experiment jointly organized by the Hubei Cotton Improvement Committee and cotton farmers in Yanglinzhou near Xiantao Town, Ganyang County this year, 'Tuo Zi' cotton matures earlier than 'Ai Zi' cotton and has a higher yield. The fiber is mostly one inch long, which is suitable for the needs of yarn mills. Before the results of variety trials are obtained, it is safer to promote this variety on a small scale. As for Chinese cotton, according to the results of the cooperative cotton planting experiment area of the Hubei Cotton Improvement Committee in Yanglinzhou this year, local farmers are very welcome to 'Million' cotton (I don't know about eastern Hubei), so it is possible to try to promote 'Million' cotton in the vicinity. As for which varieties to promote throughout the province in the future, my opinion is the same as that of Dr. Loff (the current agricultural advisor of the Ministry of Industry, who was invited by the Hubei Cotton Improvement Committee at the end of last month to come to Hubei to inspect cotton production). It is appropriate for the whole province to select five or six cotton production centers, collect famous varieties from home and abroad, and conduct regional trials for two or three years, which can prove which varieties are most suitable for promotion. Someone asked whether it is possible to purchase a large amount of cotton seeds from foreign countries and distribute them to Hubei now. I think it is impossible. I have been inspecting cotton areas in the United States for two months now and have visited a total of five cotton production experiment stations and seed companies. I know very well that even in the United States, it is impossible to obtain a large amount of purebred seeds. Most of the experimental fields have limited areas and cannot supply a large amount of purebred seeds. Even large-scale seed companies cannot purchase 1,000 dan of purebred seeds from one place. If you want a large quantity, you have to find it from the ginning mills, and the cotton seeds from the ginning mills are mostly mixed. Americans all know this. It is very dangerous to promote American varieties without first testing them in China. Therefore, even if you want to promote American cotton, you must select the most promising American cotton after three years of regional trials, import a certain amount from the United States, and propagate it in the Chinese experimental field before promoting it, which is safe and cheap. Someone also asked whether it is possible to purchase a large number of cotton seeds from its region (such as the upper reaches of the Xiang River) and promote them to other regions (such as the lower reaches of Hankou). I am very skeptical about this matter. According to this preliminary field observation, whether it is Chinese cotton or American cotton, there are currently no purebred varieties that are considered good. Mutual dissemination is nothing more than birds of a feather. How effective it will be is difficult to predict. As for permanent improvement work, it should be borne by the experimental field. The Hubei Cotton Improvement Committee's experimental general farm and two cotton seed farms are already roughly scaled and can undertake breeding and promotion work. In the future, after the establishment of the College of Agriculture of Wuhan University, the research on basic knowledge of cotton production can be undertaken by the university. Cooperation between the two parties will surely lay a solid foundation for the improvement of Chinese cotton production.
