Free Talk

New "On Teachers"

— Yu Shixia

Confucius had the saying, "One should not yield to benevolence." Teachers are indeed not entirely worthy of respect. Mencius was ridiculed for being fond of being a teacher. Teachers are also not necessarily valuable. Han Yu once claimed that there was no Zhongni in the world, so he should not be in the ranks of disciples. When discussing articles and doctrines, he solemnly regarded himself as a teacher of his generation. However, when I read his essay "On Teachers," I reached the point where I said that there is a sequence in hearing the Tao, and there are specialized studies in art. Disciples do not necessarily have to be inferior to teachers, and teachers do not necessarily have to be better than disciples. I have never doubted his grand theories and comprehensive knowledge. The Great Dai Ritual says, "There are three foundations of rituals: Heaven and earth are the foundation of life, ancestors are the foundation of lineage, and rulers and teachers are the foundation of governance." Even today, people still worship "Heaven, Earth, Ruler, Parent, Teacher," which shows how respected teachers are. Why are teachers so respected? It is because Heaven sent down the people, making them rulers and teachers. The doctrine of rulers and teachers is the reason.

In my hometown, boxing masters often do not teach their disciples all their skills, calling it "secret fist." In other hundred crafts and skills, teachers do not "leave a trick up their sleeve" for their disciples. Looking back at our own way, there are also instances of teachers and students being jealous of each other. The Forest of Language says that Ma Rong's calculation of the celestial sphere did not match, so he summoned Zheng Xuan and ordered him to calculate it once, and it was immediately determined. When Xuan completed his studies and returned home, Rong was jealous. Xuan also suspected that there were pursuers, so he sat under the bridge, with his clogs on the water. Rong indeed sent someone to pursue him. Afterwards, he told his subordinates, "Xuan is sitting on wood above the water under the earth. He will surely die." So he stopped the pursuit. If that were the case, this would be an example of a teacher being jealous of his disciple. It is said that Zhang Changshi learned Wu painting but failed and became a cursive script writer, and Yan Lugong learned Zhang's cursive script but failed and became a real script writer. These are good examples of disciples being jealous of their teachers.

Mr. Wei Mengke previously published an article in Free Talk criticizing "A Certain Society's Book Exhibition." That society then published a notice in the advertisement section of Free Talk, implying that Mengke should not lightly disparage his teacher. In my opinion, Mengke Mengjin may have words that belittle his teacher; if the person who published this notice is indeed his teacher, it seems that there is a hidden jealousy of his disciple. I do not know if Mengke will write an article to thank his teacher, as Zhang Taiyan did to Yu Quyuan, or Zhou Zuoren did to Zhang Taiyan.

On "Encirclement"

— Huaiqiu

When I was a child studying in elementary school, one day school was dismissed especially early. My father, who had never come to school, suddenly came to pick me up. I was certainly not a prodigy, although I felt that the situation was a bit different, but I didn't nervously feel that there was a serious and tense situation coming. As soon as I saw my father, I couldn't help but run up and grab his hand, while the other hand was still holding a ball. But my father didn't hug me as kindly as he did at home, and pulled me away. On the street, the people walking were still the same, but they were walking especially fast. Some people seemed to be running laps. The shops on both sides were all closed. One or two people were poking their heads out and looking through the cracks in the doors. I asked my father why the shops were closed (usually the shops only close at night), but my father didn't answer me, he just kept pulling me away. Just as we got home, my uncle told my father, "The armies of the other side of the river and Yuangia River have encircled us." (At that time, we lived in a city on the west bank of the river, and the Yuangia River was upstream). After a while, there was a burst of gunfire. We were "encircled."

That's how I learned about encirclement. Later, when I was learning about fighting at school, I often used this method of encirclement, taking sticks and bamboo strips to capture my companions' children.

This kind of encirclement with force from all directions probably existed in ancient times. I don't remember the ancient history very well, but I am familiar with the Romance of the Three Kingdoms. Liu Bei, Zhou Yu, and Cao Cao all seemed to have used this method.

Although using force to encircle can be sure of victory, it is very troublesome to mobilize troops and deploy formations. Therefore, clever modern people have opened up another path to "encirclement."

It's not necessary to cite things from a long time ago. Everyone probably still remembers the campaign to suppress the two northern warlords a few years ago. At that time, the northern army was killing its way south in a mighty manner, and although the southern army had elite troops and sufficient food, it seemed to be a bit overwhelmed. At that time, our young general was still in Shenyang, in the current puppet state of Manchukuo, observing the situation. The overwhelmed side wanted to invite him to enter the pass and implement an "encirclement." Unfortunately, the young general was quite tired of mobilizing troops. Although messengers came and went, tempting him with benefits and persuading him with righteousness, he was still lazy and not enthusiastic. In the end, the southern military advisors were厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厉he southern military advisors were厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厉he southern military advisors were厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厉he southern military advisors were厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲he southern military advisors were厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲he southern military advisors were厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厉he southern military advisors were厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厉he southern military advisors were厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厉he southern military advisors were厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厉he southern military advisors were厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲he southern military advisors were厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲he southern military advisors were厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厉he southern military advisors were厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厉he southern military advisors were厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厉he southern military advisors were厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厉he southern military advisors were厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厉he southern military advisors were厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厉he southern military advisors were厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厉he southern military advisors were厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厲害厉

After we decided to resist Japan for a long time, quite a few important or secondary Japanese figures came to China to "visit" or "visit old friends." Recently, even more have been going south and north. Although they are not going as a "full team," the total number of these few times and those few times is quite considerable. The Japanese are always good at imitating. Could it be that our secret encirclement method has been learned by them and they want to use it to encircle us once?

Breakout

— Shi Zhicun

(1) Whenever I write argumentative articles when I am emotional, I always feel good when I write them, but I inevitably regret them after they are published. I have never had a "meaningless" or "meaningful" argument with anyone. Unfortunately, "Free Talk" provoked my first emotional article. After it was published, I felt a little regret. Although I am nearly middle-aged, I still hate that my childishness has not been shed. But I have been silent until today. Counting the articles about me that I have cut out, from Mr. Gao Zhi's "Knowing Characters and Using Characters" to Mr. Feng Zhiyu's "Correcting Errors in Vain," there are already more than a dozen. Glued on a book, they can actually become a "Collection of Encirclement." I am like a prisoner who has been imprisoned for literary crimes, reading the newspaper every day in the dark prison cell about my crimes. Today, I can't help but want to break out of prison. I am a little unwilling to be surrounded by those literary formations that are besieging me, so I want to break out. Hence, I write "Breakout."

Right: Title Explanation

(2) When I was filling out the questionnaire for the Dawan Newspaper, I was thinking about the fact that we don't have enough single characters. For example, when we translate foreign books, there are many words that we often can't translate. When we look up X Han Dictionary, we often find annotations like "the square wood on the beam," "the horizontal wood between the windows," and "the appearance of a slow-flowing stream." If there is no appropriate Chinese word or phrase to translate, it is often redundant. Also, we often need to use many synonymous adjectives or verbs in a passage, and we suffer if our vocabulary is not large enough. Because of this motivation, with my ignorance, I wrote a "Literary Anthology." I certainly believe that there are many characters or words in the "Literary Anthology" that can be reapplied in our vernacular writing. As for those characters that really cannot be revived, I admit that they are already dead. As for the book "Zhuangzi," I personally like it very much. It uses all kinds of metaphors to express a meaning. Young people who want to learn to write the best explanatory writing can really learn a little from this book. The above is my original intention in daring to recommend "Zhuangzi and the Literary Anthology," but of course I cannot say separately that "Zhuangzi" is the grammar for writing and the "Literary Anthology" is the reader.

Also, I once introduced the three books "Analects," "Mencius," and "Yan's Family Instructions" to young people to learn about moral cultivation. I couldn't find a book that I could completely accept from the first word to the last word to introduce to young people. Every book has suitable and unsuitable parts. I think these three books are generally still worth reading, especially "Yan's Family Instructions." Yan Zhitui's views are not pedantic, nor is he an unreachable moralist. When I read his "Family Instructions," I never feel as bitter as when I read "Mr. Zhu Bailu's Family Management Proverbs," so I also hope that young people will read it.

On the form in the Dawan Newspaper, I also filled in two books. One is an English book, "Principles of Literary Criticism," a work by Professor Licharts, who advocates experimental criticism from a psychological analysis perspective; and the other is "Buddha's Biography," a biography. These two book titles were filled in the "Books I am Reading Now" column, not to introduce to others.

Right: I have stated my original intentions

(3) Mr. Gao Zhi's article explained four opinions: (1) "Middle school students' vocabulary is small, it is not necessarily because they know few characters... Knowing many characters does not necessarily mean that they will use them." (2) We recognize many vocabularies sometimes for reading ancient books... It does not necessarily have to be expressed in the article." (3) Today's articles are gradually adopting foreign methods. (4) Instead of having middle school students read Zhuangzi and the Literary Anthology, it is better to use this effort on the training of thought and concepts and the increase of new knowledge.

Regarding the first point, I also think so, but conversely, we cannot say, "Knowing more characters does not necessarily mean that they will use them, so there is no need to know more characters." For example, if someone knows a hundred characters, he must be able to use one or two before he knows the one hundred and first character. This is unreasonable. Another example is Mr. Shen Congwen. He has read extensively and knows four thousand characters, but when he writes novels, he uses only three thousand characters. If Mr. Gao Zhi does not read the books that Mr. Shen Congwen read, but only reads Mr. Shen Congwen's books, then he knows three thousand characters, and he will use two thousand characters. How can this be? The same is true for vocabulary and writing. When I talk about young people, I am referring to young people who can read "Zhuangzi and the Literary Anthology," not just middle school students. If I say middle school students, then junior high school students are not enough to talk about this, and there should be several senior high school students who can be counted in.

Regarding the second point, I think it should be changed: "We have become knowledgeable because we have read ancient books. Although it does not necessarily have to be expressed in the article, it can be applied when it is needed."

Regarding the third point, I still don't quite understand it. Does it mean that after an article adopts foreign methods, even the words become foreign words?

Regarding the fourth point, I have nothing to say either. I did not say that young people who read "Zhuangzi and the Literary Anthology" will eat endlessly for the rest of their lives and benefit infinitely, and do not need to seek new knowledge.

Right: Reply to Mr. Gao Zhi (to be continued)

Letters from Readers

To the editor of Free Talk:

Because I am in Beiping, it is very difficult for me to see your magazine. I am not very familiar with the situation of Shanghai writers and scholars. I have heard friends talk about it, and they always talk about it, saying that there is an article in your magazine that refers to my criticism of Zheng Zhenduo's Literary History published in the sixth issue of the fourth volume of New Moon. I regret very much that I have not been able to read this article. It is said that the content of this article says that my criticisms are not very wrong, but the attitude is very bad. Shichang is not sensitive and does not know himself. I do not know which points in my article are referred to as bad. If the author of the article can specifically point out and explain why it is worse than other book reviews, or how I should say it to be better, Shichang will be grateful. This is one thing. It is also said that a certain newspaper article said that I have surrendered to Mr. Zheng, which made people laugh at first, and then lose their smiles. Those who are shocked are shocked by the sharpness of a person's pen, who can also fabricate things out of nothing from an irresistible reason. Those who laugh laugh at their hard work and incompetence, and have nothing to do after eating. I think it is far better to take a walk on the Bund or help a coolie push a wheelbarrow, which is also a good thing. But I think this is not without reason, and I should explain it. After my manuscript was published, Mr. Zheng immediately sent a letter to the editor of New Moon, defending five points, only the last half point of which was reasonable (and this last point is the least important one-fifth of my article, as can be seen by reviewing the original text). And this last point of defense is said to have been written by a certain professor. I have rebuttals to all five points, which are more than 5,000 words long and sent to the editor of New Moon. Unfortunately, the eighth issue of the fourth volume of New Moon has not been published until now. Everyone who has a manuscript in this issue is dying of anxiety, and it is not only Shichang who is suffering. The first, third, and fourth volumes of Mr. Zheng's Literary History have been published, and I also have a long review, which I originally planned to send to New Moon, so I put it on hold. I am a very simple person. Although I grew up in Jiangnan, I have never (and do not like to) seen that kind of world in Shanghai. If I have an opinion on a certain book, I criticize it, but based on the common reason of mankind, he should believe me if he is right, and he should believe me if I am right. There is only right and wrong between us, there is no so-called "face," "attack," "surrender," or "compromise," which are only vulgar nouns that exist in vulgar brains. In Beiping, I also heard many rumors that I thought were very clever, such as a certain faction using someone to attack a certain faction, etc. Alas, if you have never been used by others or used others, how can you know that there is a noun called "use" in heaven and earth? But I ignored those rumors, so the makers of the rumors also blushed and cooled down. In fact, Mr. Zheng is a professor at Yenching, and I am a student. We meet every day, and sometimes eat together. If he has a book in the future, I can still criticize each other if I have an opinion. If we find the truth, we can admit it to each other. I have been reading books for more than ten years, and I have not read these kinds of nouns of "surrender" and "compromise." Which gentleman gave them to me? I return them to you with a long bow here. If the editor is kind enough to publish this letter, my gratitude will be inexpressible. Best wishes. Wu Shichang

Two Brothers (12)

— Authored by Maupassant, Translated by Li Weike

Notary Public Lecaru continued,

"My colleague in Paris has already notified me of the main provisions of his will. In that will, he specifies your son, Jean Roland, as the heir to all his property."

Everyone was so surprised by these words that they couldn't say a word.

Madame Roland was the first to restrain her emotions, saying haltingly,

"Oh my, poor René... our poor friend... Oh my... Oh my... He's dead!..."

Tears appeared in her eyes, the quiet tears of a woman, so painful and yet so clear as they flowed down her cheeks, drops of sorrow emanating from the soul.

But Old Man Roland was completely focused on the joyful news of the inheritance, not caring about the death of his old friend. However, he dared not immediately inquire about the terms of the will and the amount of the property. To get to these relevant questions, he circled around and asked,

"What disease did poor Maréchal die of?"

Mr. Lecaru did not know this at all. He said,

"I only know that the deceased had no direct heirs. He left all his property! An annual interest of about 20,000 francs attached to a 3% debt! All of it is left to your second son, saying that he watched him being born, growing up, and considered him suitable to receive this bequest. If Mr. Jean does not wish to accept it, the inheritance will be donated to the foundlings in the orphanage." Old Man Roland could no longer hide his joy, he exclaimed,

"Great! This is truly a kind thought. If I had no descendants, I would never forget to bequeath my property to this honest friend!"

The notary smiled and said,

"I was very happy to report this matter to you in person. Bringing good news to people is always a joy."

He had no idea that this good news was the death of a friend, the death of one of Old Man Roland's best friends, and Roland himself quickly forgot the close friendship he had just described so precisely.

Only Madame Roland and her two children maintained a sorrowful expression. She was still weeping softly, dabbing her eyes with a handkerchief, and then placing the handkerchief over her mouth to suppress the heavy sighs.

The doctor said softly,

"He was an honest and very kind man. He often invited us to dinner, me and my brother."

Jean's eyes were wide open and sparkling with excitement. With a practiced gesture, he held his beautiful golden beard in his right hand, stroking it all the way to the tips of the longest strands, as if to lengthen and thin them out. (To be continued)

US President's Reiteration of Prices Stirred Cotton Market Reaction

New York, 27th Report on Cotton Market in One Week, President Roosevelt's renewed attention to raising prices and establishing the gold market declaration, stirred up the cotton market reaction, but all the needs were for hedging and long closing. Therefore, the weekend market situation slightly declined. Those in the industry have conflicting views on the impact of raising gold prices on the price level. The deposit of one angle per pound has been implemented in the South, and it is said that its foundation is quite stable, although some farmers who signed the contract are quite skeptical. It is reported that the cotton contract, which destroyed cotton fields this year, and the rent paid by the government, will be distributed in the middle of next week. The exchange of Indian raw cotton and Japanese goods has attracted much attention. At the same time, the resumption of diplomatic relations between the United States and Russia will increase a source of exports for American cotton, which is also very noteworthy.

Grain Slightly Improved Far-Month Flour

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the market for each month showed a trend of stabilizing first and then weakening. As the Chicago quotation for foreign wheat rebounded by about one dollar and one dime, and Canada rose by one or two dimes, people's confidence was still stable at the beginning. Later, due to the successive return of actual sales brokers, the spot price in Tianjin showed a flat and weak trend. The exchange's previous restrictions on sellers were announced to the market the day before yesterday, restoring the original state. In this way, manufacturers gained the convenience of selling again. For this reason, although the price of foreign wheat rebounded, the market atmosphere turned quiet again, about one cent less than the previous day. By the afternoon opening, the market was very soft for this month due to a large number of returned draft orders. The forward contracts recovered as many firms frequently bought them in, but there were few transactions, just a small rebound. As a result, October and November each rose by a small five mills, December by a large seven and a half mills, January by a large one and a half cents, and February and March by a large one cent.

Wheat Market Gradually Stabilizing

Yesterday's futures wheat market generally showed a stable trend. As the quotation for foreign wheat rebounded, people's confidence did not fluctuate much after the opening. However, as the spot chips on the market gradually decreased, foreign wheat seemed unable to arrive immediately. Moreover, considering the situation this month (with about thirty vehicles for actual delivery), although the market has ended, the final rebound was absorbed by manufacturers. The industry and outsiders generally viewed it as such, and the market atmosphere gradually stabilized. As a result, November and December each improved by one cent, January by two cents, February by three cents, and March by two cents. The current wheat still appears stable, with the opening price for Bengbu wheat at three yuan and nine dimes and a half, Jiangyan wheat at three yuan and eight dimes and six or seven cents, Gaoyou wheat at three yuan and eight dimes and five cents, and Wuhu wheat at three yuan and five dimes and seven cents, with Fuxin taking away five thousand packages and Fufeng taking away one thousand packages, it is said.

A total of forty-five vehicles of spot wheat were delivered this month, with No. 1 taking away thirty vehicles, and the rest being sporadic hoarding and arbitrage income.

Silk and Tea The Drastic Change in US Exchange Rate Affects Silk Prices

(New York Silk Prices Plummeted by More Than One Dime) After the United States announced its policy of raising prices, the US exchange rate gradually contracted. The New York raw silk market price gradually rose by one dime, five or six cents per pound (US dollars). However, the exchange market suddenly underwent a drastic reaction the day before yesterday. The exchange rate plummeted, and the silk price also plummeted accordingly, falling by more than one dime per pound (US dollars), returning to the original price before the increase. The sudden rise and fall of silk prices in New York this time was purely due to the exchange rate relationship, and silk sales remained sluggish. (Sixty More Pieces of Sichuan Yellow Silk Arrived) Yesterday, the Jiangshun轮船 imported sixty pieces of Sichuan yellow silk, which were loaded from Hankou and taken back to the warehouse by Baotaihe and others for storage.

(Artificial Silk Sales Continue to Be Flat) Yesterday, the local artificial silk market continued to be flat. Only the Changjiang gang imported 28 boxes of Shuangxing, Honglv, and Jinzhong brands for November futures, priced from 172 yuan and five dimes to 170 yuan and seven dimes and a half net.

(Silk Sales in Shanghai Stalled Again) Overseas silk prices have been gradually rising for several days due to exchange rates. However, the US exchange rate soared the day before yesterday, and New York silk prices plummeted by more than thirty yuan in one day (Chinese currency per package). However, Lyon in the UK was still able to stand firm. Shanghai's major US firms, hearing of this exchange change, did not dare to take risks, and the market was stagnant. There was only a half-day market yesterday morning, and there were no transactions in current silk. The future of silk sales is still difficult to grasp for a while.

The selling price of Gaoghuang goods from Wuyuan North Road ranged from 116 yuan to 129 yuan. The selling price of Tunxi goods ranged from 90 yuan to 105 yuan. Oil Market New Tallow From West Zhejiang Is Approaching

New tallow goods are about to appear, and those engaged in this industry are paying attention to the buying and selling of new oil. Shanghai is adjacent to Zhejiang Province, and especially close to the production area of Jiaxing in West Zhejiang. Therefore, the earliest arrival of new oil in Shanghai every year should be the Ben Che oil from Jiaxing. Because pressing is already underway around the Light Snow period in that area, once new oil is seen, it can arrive in the local area overnight. If measured by past years, then the sales of futures have already been traded at this time. However, the candle-making industry and Taobao merchants are used to prepare for the New Year's goods. According to the lunar calendar, it is still in the early ninth month, and the preparation for the New Year's goods is still far away. Therefore, the candle merchants' attitude is quite calm. However, according to the season, the tallow seeds have already matured, and the pressing workshops in the production area are busy collecting seeds and pressing oil. It is said that the harvest in West Zhejiang is still good, and the old oil has just been sold out, continuing the new goods without interruption. According to the situation in Zhejiang Road, new oil seems difficult to be too cheap. Moreover, the Shaoxing pressing workshops have already been buying tallow seeds in the Jiaxing area for sales, and the price is generally between five yuan and five or six dimes per stone. Calculated on this basis, the cost of tallow oil may be more than twenty yuan. Currently, local industry insiders estimate that it is only within twenty yuan, because there are still many old goods of Hanjing Jingma oil, etc., which has led to a gradual market weakness. The Shanghai market has always followed the lead of the Hankou market. For this reason, it has not been able to approach Zhejiang Road, and the tallow seed pressing workshops in West Zhejiang have not yet collected the seeds and dare not rashly sell oil at a low price, resulting in a quiet new market in the market these days. In short, the start of pressing this year is earlier, and each family must prepare more of the raw material tallow seeds, so the price of seeds may not be easy to expect to be cheap. And the oil output will increase compared with previous years, so the oil price is not easy to be good. In the future, raw goods and cooked goods may go in opposite directions, which is also unknown. If that is the case, then the operation of each pressing workshop will be very difficult to cope with. The local industry's base accumulation is already thin, but sales are extremely scattered, and it is generally waiting for the development of new goods. The cargo price of Chong Jing is still around twenty-two yuan per burden, Ping Jing is twenty-one yuan and three or four dimes, and Macheng is nineteen yuan and five or six dimes. Although the Hankou market is stable on the surface, the content is extremely miserable, and the market is quite depressed.

Spring and Autumn

Special Issue School Life

Newcomer Key

— Ji Jue

I remember that one year, I visited an opening ceremony at a certain church university. One of the programs was the presentation of the "Newcomer Key" to the representative of the freshman class by the class leader of the sophomore class. The program was very solemn and tense. The so-called "key" was actually a long key, and the word "newcomer" was directly translated from the English "Freshman". The key was engraved with the four characters "Gate of Entering Virtue", meaning that it was the key to entering virtue for university freshmen. They could keep it for one year, and after one year, they would pass it on to the next class of freshmen, circulating between the old and the new. This program has therefore been followed to this day.

For a group of students who have just come out of the orderly and constrained middle school and stepped into the complex threshold of the university, without understanding the mystery of university life and without fully understanding the search for the treasure trove of knowledge, this golden key to enlighten and stimulate is given to prevent them from blindly rushing around without a clue, hoping that they will move towards the "Gate of Entering Virtue". After one year, whether they have entered the "Gate of Entering Virtue" is still a question, but this mysterious key must be passed on to the next class of students. The next class of students will even more obediently "draw a gourd according to the pattern".

Things in society often evolve in this way. The advanced generations can earnestly exhort the younger generations to work hard and instruct them on the methods of dealing with people and things. The younger generations do not follow his exhortations, completely abandoning all the wise sayings left by the advanced generations, doing whatever they want, making human desires rampant, and the society becomes more and more chaotic. As a result, the predecessors' last words are passed on to future generations in their original form, still calling on them to learn well, but the fact may not be so! Mr. Sun Yat-sen devoted himself to the revolution for forty years, knowing that "the revolution has not yet succeeded", and earnestly instructed future generations with "comrades still need to work hard". Those who died after Mr. Sun Yat-sen must apologetically say "the revolution has not succeeded but the body has died first...work hard! Comrades..."

But I hope that this is not comparable to the story of the "Newcomer Key".

Monday Morning

— Shu Ying

The clock on the wall of the No. room is pointing to eight o'clock. The gatekeeper, Afu, is printing lecture notes on the mimeograph machine. At this time, he looks up at the clock and wants to walk out the door, but suddenly seems to realize something, stops, and turns back to continue his work.

Class begins and ends, and the bell rings on time. This is the gatekeeper's responsibility. If he is late, he will be scolded, especially for the bell that ends class. However, every Monday, the first class is usually a memorial week, which will only be held after the principal arrives, so ringing the bell cannot be as monotonous as on weekdays.

The playground, a small square surrounded by high walls, is already bathed in sunlight, and the air is relatively warmer. Except for those in the dormitory, all the students are gathered here. Some are playing ball, some are doing woolen work, and some are holding books to read, but most are talking:

"How did you have fun yesterday?" Ms. C asked several classmates standing with her.

"The three of us watched a movie at the Nanjing Grand Theater. How about you?"

"Yesterday there were many guests at my house, so I just muddled through the day at home. In the evening, B asked me to go dancing. I think dancing is more interesting."

"Of course! But we who live in the school don't have this blessing, and we don't have such a limelight as you, and no one accompanies us."

"Don't make fun of me, but it's okay to go even if you live in the school. Yesterday I saw the principal and Mr. T there, and it was already past eleven o'clock when they went. I was afraid that we would all be restrained, so I left first. I really wasn't satisfied!"

Little sister D looked at her watch at this time:

"Oh my god! It's going to die, it's already half past nine, how long will we have to wait! I'm afraid he danced until dawn last night and is still sleeping now."

"Who cares, isn't it good to bask in the sun here a little longer?"

"That's right, I don't think there's any point in going to class. These teachers are really incompetent," Ms. A said somewhat conceitedly.

"Dang! Dang! Dang!" Afu rang the bell so loudly that it shook the sky, and the atmosphere suddenly became tense. Everyone gradually walked to the auditorium, which was filled in an instant. First, everyone stood up, saluted, and sang. When the chairman respectfully read the will of the Premier, the principal appeared on the stage, faced the portrait, and read the will aloud. After reading it, he bowed his head in silence. From the back, he looked very pious.

"Report!" As soon as this voice came out, Principal quickly turned around and gave everyone a slight nod with a kind smile, and began to report, the gist of which was: "The national crisis is so serious, and the Japanese are bullying us so much, I hope that the students will all take on the responsibility of saving the country." Then the director of discipline, the director of education, and the director of affairs successively reported on school affairs, gave lectures, etc. Everyone became impatient to listen, the sound of talking rose, and the woolen work was openly taken out and done.

Time passed minute by minute, and the stage was finally empty, and then the meeting was dismissed.

Afu is really too obsequious. As soon as people walked into the classroom, he rang the class bell again.

As soon as Mr. Huang walked into the classroom door, everyone shouted:

"Hey! The third class is about to end, why are we still having the second class?"

"We don't want your teachers to teach!"

"It's better to have it tomorrow, there will be one tomorrow, it's already over today."

Mr. Huang seemed unwilling to leave, and while they were at an impasse, the old Mr. Yu of Chinese came.

"I'm sorry! I'm sorry!" The old gentleman greeted Mr. Huang and said.

"Don't be polite!" Mr. Huang took his book and walked out.

Then there was a roar of laughter.

The Chinese teacher is the best at talking, so the laughter continued for a long time, and no one heard the roll call.

Sketches of University Dormitories

— Luo Cun Ren

There are three people in the same room: Lao Zhang, Lao Wang, and Lao Li.

Today, Lao Zhang's leather shoes could be heard from far away as he came to the room, especially hurried and powerful. As soon as he arrived in the room, he slammed the lecture notes, which were only assigned a few chapters to look at during the big exam, onto the table with a whoosh. The head of the lecture notes was already crisscrossed with the names and criticisms of female students, which was the result of discussing with Lao Zhao next door during class.

At this time, Lao Wang's love letter had just been written. There was no more work to do, so he wanted to ask Lao Zhang for news.

"Lao Zhang, did you Make eyes with Xiao Zhou in class today?"

"Why not, I'm telling you, she seems to have a little interest too. She didn't turn her head to look at me a few days ago."

After Lao Zhang said this, he was happy and a little embarrassed. He wanted to cover up this embarrassment, so he became happy with Lao Wang. He laughed and suddenly hugged Lao Wang, shouting madly:

"Sister, I love you!"

Who knew that the voice was too loud and woke up Lao Li, who was taking a nap. No one could guess what Lao Li was dreaming about during the day. Although his dream was awakened, Lao Li was not angry, because the topic of discussion was neither as boring as national affairs nor as rigid as academics. After listening to Lao Zhang's report on the love affair in class today, he was very excited and felt happy for others' happiness.

"That's right, Lao Zhang," Lao Li said loudly to Lao Zhang, and then suggested to Lao Zhang:

"First, you go to borrow notes from her in a few days. This is both generous and not abrupt."

"And then?" Lao Zhang was anxious to death.

"Second," Lao Li said again, "aren't we going to have a department meeting soon? Let's have you two work together as committee members."

"That's right, it's good to have a committee (tail) to interact with." Lao Wang laughed, Lao Li also laughed, and Lao Zhang laughed even more. The laughter of the three people turned a room into a pond full of frogs.

Hahahaha!

Dangers of Off-Campus Dormitories

— Sun Zongwen

The value of land and rent in Shanghai is really too expensive, so many schools cannot build more dormitories to accommodate students' boarding. Some students have to rent dormitories near the school on their own. However, apartment-style buildings in Shanghai that are exclusively for students are currently in the minority, so they have to live with ordinary people, and various dangerous things happen from then on.

I often hear friends say: "What is the reason for this? Many young people go to Shanghai to study, and as a result, they end up 'unable to return to their hometown' and 'unable to see their parents'..." At first, I couldn't figure out why. Now I think what I'm about to say may be one reason, one fact.

In the dormitories outside of XX school, there are some students whose actions now I dare not assert that they will definitely fall in the future, but these actions are indeed enough to lead young people to the road of depravity, which is very assertive.

Playing mahjong, playing cards... These are all the worst pastimes in society, which is admitted by many. But now these students not only cannot persuade people to improve, but instead do it themselves with relish. Every night, you can always hear the sound of playing cards and dice in their rooms. It's even worse on Sundays. Everything, they are really too interested in these gambling activities.

The purpose of gambling is nothing more than to use money to win or lose, but students' money is limited. If the money runs out, I am afraid that at that time, all kinds of dangerous actions will unconsciously arise!

During this national crisis, what are the responsibilities of students? What should be done? What should not be done. I think very smart students will definitely be able to wake up; but now these students are too blinded by bad habits, and without great courage, I am afraid they will not be able to run out of the dangerous den of all evil!

Alas! Sin! Dormitory outside XX school.

Two Geography Teachers

— Yan

Recently, I heard two geography teachers' absolutely different views on Chinese geography teaching, and they were arguing so ridiculously and painfully.

A said: When I teach students Chinese geography, after the signing of the Tanggu Truce, I will never talk about the four northeastern provinces, because these four provinces are no longer ours. Although the government is shouting about long-term resistance, it is actually a long-term betrayal; the anti-Japanese heroes say that they will continue to fight, but in fact they are in long-term recuperation; suppressing the outside and pacifying the inside has become harmonizing with the outside and pacifying the inside. There is no hope of recovering these fallen four provinces, so every time I mention them, I feel infinitely sad, like losing a treasure, and there is no hope of returning the pearl. The more I think about it, the more sad I am, but it is useless to be sad and useless to be sad. What we should pay attention to now are the mountains and rivers of the unlost land, and the population, products, transportation, politics, industry and commerce, education, etc., should all be made clear to the students, so that they know their relationship with life, and arouse their love for this beautiful country, so that they cannot bear to lose another inch of land. It is also like taking out the unlost treasures and instructing the children and grandchildren one by one, telling them their functions and values, calling on them to preserve them forever and pass them on forever, so that they will never be lost again. Isn't this better than just hurting the lost land and actually having no power to recover it? Therefore, my not talking about the four northeastern provinces is precisely to protect the unlost land.

B said: In the past, when talking about the four northeastern provinces, it could be brief and sloppy, but now it must be taught more thoroughly. The area and population of the four provinces, railways and rivers, sorghum and soybeans, forests and minerals, animal skins and wool, high mountains and plains, wasteland and cultivated land, and the relationship between these four provinces and the whole country, etc., must all be made more familiar and more recognized by the students, so that they can feel the pain of loss and strengthen their determination to recover it. It is like losing a treasure. The more I think about it, the more I feel its loveliness, and the more I try to recover it, and I worry and think hard. Over time, I can naturally return the pearl to Hepu. The government does not want to recover the four northeastern provinces, don't we want to call on the students of the future to recover them? Therefore, my speaking of the four northeastern provinces is more important now than in the past, precisely to prepare for the recovery of the lost land, and also to preserve the whole country.

Is it not ridiculous to not read about the lost territory? Is it not also painful? Speaking vaguely and briefly before losing it, knowing to pay attention to it after it is lost, is it not also the same ridiculous and painful?

Shen Bao Amateur Weekly

Look! The Current State of Our Countryside

— Gong Pu

Not long ago, I, the reporter, received a letter from a friend in the rural area of Xieshi, Zhejiang. It described the bankruptcy of the Chinese rural economy with the following passage:

"I have personally witnessed the bankruptcy of the rural economy and the general plight of the peasants here. Taxes remain high without reduction, and the prices of agricultural products are generally low. The vast majority of farmers are consciously expressing many subconscious complaints about the current situation. These voices can be easily heard on small boats on the inland rivers, in teahouses, and at gatherings under the mulberry trees in the fields. Without even asking, one can hear the same discussions, curses, and protests. However, they are very scattered and unorganized!"

Following this, at the end of his letter, there is a quote from an old farmer that is even more thought-provoking and enlightening for us to understand the crisis and direction of improvement for this Chinese nation that relies on agriculture:

"Yesterday, an old farmer answered me with the following words, which I feel carry a very serious meaning. He said: 'We have the fields, and we haven't sold a single piece of them. We have never been lazy in our lives (referring to work). But this year, it's as if the fields are gone, our hard work is in vain, and we are inexplicably poor!' Finally, he added vaguely and self-pityingly: 'But we will never believe that we made ourselves poor!'" This is the situation for a self-cultivating farmer; the bankruptcy situation is already like this. Then, the miserable situation of other general hired farmhands can be imagined. Here, the land price was worth 100 yuan per mu two years ago, but now no one is interested even at 40 yuan."

Such complaints are still limited to the relatively wealthy rural areas of Jiangsu and Zhejiang. As for the general bankruptcy of the rural economies in provinces such as Anhui, Hubei, Henan, Shaanxi, Gansu, and Sichuan, the situation is even more significant. According to a recent report received by the Shanghai General Office of the Red Swastika Society from the Commissioner for Disaster Relief in northern Anhui, the devastation of the rural areas around Yingfu and Taihe in northern Anhui, with bandits everywhere, is truly astonishing. It is said that in recent years, due to the declining rural economy in various parts of northern Anhui, the old and weak sit and wait for death, while the young and strong often take risks and join the ranks of bandits. This time, as many as twenty-five towns around Yingfu were burned and looted by bandits, and more than 8,000 people were abducted. Over one thousand people were killed at Nanzhao Market and over three thousand at the old county market of Taihe. Only a limited number were redeemed because when those who came to redeem the hostages entered the bandit territory, the bandits were numerous, and they would be checked in each group. If they carried money, it would be searched and taken away, regardless of whether they were there to redeem hostages or not. After the money was taken away, they would cry and complain to that group of bandits, but that group would think it was a lie, or cut off their ears or hands, and still let them go back to raise money, threatening to kill them if they did not meet the deadline. All the children, those who were eight years old were tied in a string, those who were nine or ten years old were tied in a string, and those who were over ten years old were tied in a string, all connected with hemp ropes, and whipped from behind, making them wail and jump. The bandits enjoyed this. Such a tragic scene, not to mention witnessing it personally, is unbearable to imagine just hearing about it! And what we should especially know is that the so-called Yingfu and Taihe areas were the most prosperous agricultural areas in northern Anhui ten years ago. Yingfu (Fuyang) is the old Yingzhou Prefecture city. Taihe is about one hundred li from Fuyang, both being large towns along the Ying River, a tributary of the Huai River, about five hundred li from Bengbu. Ten years ago, British and American merchants purchased more than one million yuan worth of agricultural products, such as eggs, pigs, and cattle, every year in this area, transported them from the Ying River to Bengbu, loaded them onto the Jinpu Railway, transferred them to Yangtze River steamers, and exported them to Shanghai. The prosperity of that place at that time can be imagined. Who would have thought that ten years later, it would be reduced to this state?

Let's look at Sichuan again! According to people who recently came from Sichuan, "The current state of rural abandonment in that province is far beyond imagination. The main reason is that the warlords in Sichuan have been engaged in endless infighting for several years, coupled with droughts. The land tax in northern Sichuan has been collected up to the year 260 of the Republic of China, that is, pre-collected for 240 years in advance. Although the southern, eastern, and western parts of Sichuan have not reached this level, they have at least been collected up to the years 60 or 70 of the Republic of China, that is, 40 or 50 years in advance! Therefore, the people all regard engaging in honest work as foolish. Everyone indulges in gambling, and all the parks and entertainment venues have been replaced by gambling dens!"

We hear about the trend of the entire rural collapse in various inland provinces, and we see the situation of all the abnormally developing things on the surface in Shanghai. Unless we don't use our brains to think, we believe that we don't have to wait for imperialism to take action themselves. This huge Republic of China is about to hand itself over to others for joint management and division! Don't believe it? Look! Everything that has been expressed in various aspects recently, isn't every single one of them heading down this road?

The progress of a society, and even the revival of an entire nation, depends on the struggle of various forces in all aspects, constantly moving forward, in order to achieve results. Looking at the current situation, apart from a few people who are self-righteous and blindly and chaotically acting, making bombastic statements to deceive people, what shows this kind of struggling power? This entire society has entered a state of complete lifelessness! This is the feeling that reality gives us; it's not a question of pessimism or optimism.

Eye Exercises Before Watching the Tide

— Sha Shelang

Factory Worker... Small Clerk

"Ahem!" I knew it was him again when I heard that sound. I quickly took those few pages of invoices from the drawer and placed them on the table, ready to judge by his expression. At the same time, my heart was beating.

"Have you finished calculating?" he asked, with an impatient expression and a strong tone.

I stood up and handed him those few pages of invoices, but the reply that came to my throat, I swallowed it down again.

"Six, seven, eight! Hey, I want to see the invoices for September."

"Sir, the invoices for September haven't been finalized yet."

"What! Haven't been finalized yet? You handle things really... really..."

His eyeballs, separated by three hundred degrees of "Zeiss" glass, popped up, almost rolling out. A thin smile floated on his nose, what an embarrassing expression. But I pretended to be upright, standing and waiting for his next words...

"Why don't you finalize them quickly? Don't you know that the manager is urging for the general ledger? The manager... you have to understand. Don't hold me back."

"Yes! Sir, the September inventory ledger was originally finalized, but the machine parts list from the coppersmith foreman hasn't been checked and sent over..."

"No, annoying. I don't care about your coppersmith foreman or anyone else. I only ask you for the September invoices."

"Yes... yes... sir, but if there is no machine parts list, there is nowhere to check the prices of many things."

"According to what you say, then you will never finalize it? Why don't you urge him?"

"Yes... yes, but, I have already urged him. The coppersmith foreman said that the general ledger will be submitted to the manager at the end of the month..."

At this time, it felt like a hundred fawns were running in my heart, and ten million needles were pricking my back. The air in front of me was suffocating. He said seriously again, "What do you know? Too troublesome, you go sit in my seat. You young people are most hateful for not obeying the orders of your superiors. To be honest with you, obeying your superiors is never wrong."

He threw it lightly on my desk with his hand, half to express his anger, and the other half seemed to express that his words were absolute.

"Yes, yes, yes..." I dare not say anything more. Secretly peeking at his eyes that had not calmed down.

"No, you can't stay here. I'll wait for your September invoices."

Fortunately, the coppersmith foreman sent the machine parts list.

Current Affairs Research

On Germany's Withdrawal from the League of Nations

— Ms. Zhao Xianjing

Many people have expressed boundless sympathy and admiration for Hitler's withdrawal from the League of Nations this time, believing that this is the most concrete manifestation of oppressed nations resisting the united oppression of international imperialism. If the issue is really that simple, then wasn't Japan's withdrawal from the League not long ago also a manifestation of resisting imperialism? The withdrawal of any country from the League of Nations is of course due to dissatisfaction with the League of Nations and the League of Nations' inability to grant certain rights, and it is definitely not without purpose. Therefore, to conclude that a country's break from the constraints of the League of Nations is resistance to imperialism would be laughably foolish in thought!

If China were the one withdrawing from the League of Nations this time, that would be a joyful action of resisting imperialism because China is in a colonial position. However, Germany is different from and even the opposite of China. Before the war, Germany was the overlord of imperialism. After the war, although it was in the position of a defeated country and suffered the oppression of the victorious countries, struggling under the Treaty of Versailles, there is no doubt that it is still an imperialist country from its domestic and foreign political and economic relations. And Hitler's rise to power is further proof that Germany is moving toward the peak of imperialism. Therefore, Hitler's withdrawal from the international organization this time because he could not achieve his demand for equal armaments is precisely an expression of the irreconcilable contradictions between imperialists. Where is the anti-imperialist action of the German nation?

Indeed, the external appearance of the German National Socialist Party, in short, is extreme nationalism, state supremacy. Its political goal is to thoroughly develop the spirit of militarism externally, oppose the Treaty of Versailles; and internally, it loathes Marxism and negates class struggle. Therefore, before it gained power, its slogan was to build Greater Germany, abolish the Treaty of Versailles, and oppose socialist parties. Taking advantage of the increasingly deepening economic panic, political instability, and the leftist thinking of the working class and peasants, Hitler seized power by the fastest means and sat on the throne of German rule. However, he is very clear that under the current situation, it is impossible to refuse the support of various imperialists and rule Germany and suppress the "reactionaries" alone. Especially the contradictions and weakness of the National Socialist Party itself made him express softening to international imperialism on the first day after he gained power, saying: "The new cabinet maintains peaceful and friendly relations with the world." And the "abolition of the Treaty of Versailles," which was originally one of the main political programs of the National Socialist Party, was silently changed to "amend the Treaty of Versailles." As for his four-year plan to revive Germany, it is still an unfulfilled check to this day. All of this is enough to make the German people's belief in Hitler waver day by day. Therefore, in order to extend the life of his rule, Hitler took the opportunity of the resumption of the Disarmament Conference to put forward the demand for equal armaments. When his request was not fulfilled, he followed it up with withdrawal from the League of Nations, wanting to divert the line of sight of domestic opposition with foreign issues. However, Hitler only issued a notice of withdrawal from the League of Nations. The actual restraints have not yet been lifted, but he triumphantly erected a so-called "Liberation Monument" in Kelheim and publicly gave a speech: Germany's only purpose is to seek happiness and love peace, so now they have nothing to ask for but to work with peace of mind! It can be seen that Hitler's withdrawal from the League of Nations this time is not to revive Germany from the extreme nationalist standing, he is just representing the higher-class Germans or German imperialists to express surrender or non-resistance to other imperialists.

In a panic　emotion, even dialing the abacus beads became strangely inflexible. Awkwardly, I calculated five times and got five totals. My brain was tired enough from the surveillance of authority. I believed in myself that normally my calculation wouldn't be so bad.

"Gosh, your calculation, hehe, your calculation." These taunts were enough for me to endure. I only hated that there was no hole in the ground to hide in. My feet felt like they had paralysis. I didn't dare to look up at him again.

Originally, there are many such people in this society丨丨 who are unwilling to give others "guidance" and "mutual assistance," but regard "contempt" and "mockery" as their specialty.

If it weren't for the sake of life, I would definitely have run away.

The September invoices were finally settled under his supervision. When he left, he smiled sarcastically, as if mocking me, and said, "Friend, I only know today that your abilities are not bad."

What was left to me was only endless "embarrassment."

After being silent for half an hour, the subordinate clerks in the same position as me whispered again: "He urged so urgently, isn't it just because he wanted to ask for leave to see the tide!"

However, I only then realized the authority of the superior clerk.

Methods for Small Capital to Operate Small Factories

— Ben

Under the capitalist law of large capital swallowing small capital, it is originally very difficult for small capital to operate small factories, especially in Chinese society, which is externally oppressed by international imperialism and internally attacked by continuous natural and man-made disasters, making the sales market increasingly smaller. Added to the encroachment of large capital, it becomes even more difficult. However, if managed properly, I think it is not necessarily impossible to achieve considerable success. I will now describe my experience and observations below for the reference of those who have small capital and aspire to operate small factories.

(1) Choose to operate those that large capital disdains to operate and that are suitable for the environment and needs. If such industries cannot be found, then choose to operate those with relatively cheap raw materials.

(2) Obtain the secret to the sales market. Reduce prices and improve goods. Lower prices will lead to sales, and better goods will lead to more buyers.

(3) Apply machines that save time and procedures. Although such machines are relatively expensive, they can reduce workers and increase production.

(4) After the factory is opened, the size of the capital required to manufacture goods depends on the speed of sales of the manufactured goods. If you can increase the speed of sales, you can reduce the need for capital and obtain greater profits.

(5) Do not treat workers too harshly, because if they are too harsh, the workers will be dissatisfied; if the workers are dissatisfied, the products will be poor and slow. It must be known that the most important advantage of small factories competing with large factories is the harmonious cooperation between the capital and labor.

(6) Efforts should be made to enable factories or stores in the same industry to exchange opinions and content with each other, and not to strictly keep secrets from each other and destroy each other.

(7) The employment of people should be based purely on talent and ability, and all recommendations based on favors must be strictly prohibited.

(8) Industrial research and experiments should be carried out without slack, so that manufactured products can be improved at any time.

(9) Associations should be formed with the same industry for advertising and publicity.

(10) Save on overhead expenses.

The above is naturally just a few major principles; however, if you can follow these principles and add them to your own environmental position, even if you can't achieve great success, you will never fail completely!

Amateur Education

Sunday Education for Working Children in England

— Li Peiying

In Christian countries, people mostly put on clean clothes on Sundays, remove their usual hard-working faces, and happily go for a walk. This naturally refers to professional people above the middle and upper classes, but laborers have no way to enjoy it because they have to work for a living, regardless of the Sabbath. Because laborers have no time to educate their children, the church comes to serve them. Especially for working children in those so-called civilized countries, they have to go to church every Sabbath to pray. Is this because children and their fathers and brothers like religious beliefs? No! It is entirely because children can get a hearty lunch and some rest at noon when they go to church.

In Germany, the Children Protection Act prohibits children under the age of ten from participating in labor. However, according to a 1930 survey in Saxony, among 52,930 school children, 34,303 were laborers; similarly, in the Sarfeld area, 20% of school children were engaged in certain labor.

According to a recent survey, 7,895 primary school students in Berlin are engaged in illegal labor. According to class time, 633 children work 4 hours a day, 119 work 6 hours, and 1,153 cannot even rest completely on Sundays. These children not only do not get better nutrition, but even lack clothes. Especially after Hitler's dictatorship, children are almost completely plunged into a dark hell like their parents.

This phenomenon of children's hell is the same in England. In addition to eating a meal and resting in church every Sabbath, working children in England have to sing hymns, tell stories of the Heavenly Father, and read the Bible told by the clergy. However, because the laborers' children are not interested in these, the church has also set up some singing teams or sports teams to attract them. This

International Broadcasting He Lei

Ural Machine-Building Plant

— Guo Xiu Fu

After the October Revolution, the Soviet Union, in order to transform itself from the most backward agricultural country in capitalism into a socialist country surpassing capitalist industrial nations, embarked on the famous Five-Year Economic Plan. To shift all sectors of the national economy to the latest technological foundations—the foundation of the socialist machine industry and the technological base of electrification—the first Five-Year Plan saw the construction of agricultural machinery factories and the world-renowned Dnipro Hydroelectric Station. In the second Five-Year Plan, one of the biggest achievements in heavy industry during the first year was the completion of the Ural Machine-Building Plant in Sverdlovsk. This factory is vast in scale, divided into seven plants: a machine plant, an iron material manufacturing plant, a repair plant, a white iron casting plant, a copper material casting plant, a tool plant, and a model plant, with each plant further divided into many departments. The factory's main products include rolling machines and iron smelting furnaces, among others. These iron smelting furnaces are enormous machines, originally only available in the United Kingdom, the United States, and Germany. However, due to the impact of the capitalist economic panic, the 275 furnaces in the UK, 250 in the US, and 100 in Germany were successively shut down. In contrast, the Soviet Union built 275 iron smelting furnaces during the first Five-Year Plan.

Within this factory, there are forty-six types of wall newspapers (mostly dailies) and one thousand two hundred and thirty-four worker correspondents. The submissions are all about striving forward in work. Under the extensive network of correspondents, extending from the machine factory's offices to various plants and departments, public dining halls, and shops, everyone is striving for more production, better quality, improved meals, supply and demand of daily necessities, cleanliness, and hygiene.

Concise and incisive wall newspapers, under the slogan "For Building the Ural Iron Smelting Furnace Plant," greatly assisted this machine-building plant. The newspapers are filled with vivid and lively submissions from its correspondents, reflecting the difficulties, victories, and upward mobility of workers and specialists in their work. They unanimously praised the heroic men and women of the Ural Machine-Building Plant, posting photos of socialist heroes in the newspapers and encouraging other workers to strive to become heroes of socialist construction. In addition, the newspapers regularly publish workers' insights and experiences regarding their work, providing them as a reference for other workers.

Along with the factory's growth and development, many boys and girls from the countryside have undergone the baptism of new socialist culture, economics, and politics, becoming skilled workers, technicians, and organizers.

The living standards of the workers are also improving. Although Sverdlovsk has a good theater, it is inconvenient for the workers of the Ural Machine-Building Plant. Therefore, a cultural center district large enough to accommodate 60,000 people is now being built. It includes cinemas, clubs, a circus, a library, and a cultural and recreation park. Many schools are under construction, and nineteen kindergartens have been established. In addition, worker dormitories with a volume of 12,300 cubic meters have been built, each with a manager specifically responsible for the repair, renting, and cleanliness and hygiene of the rooms within the dormitory.

Page 23

Similarly, it was not until the establishment of Socialist Sunday Schools (SSS) that church education began to suffer a significant blow, as they were opponents of church education.

Socialist Sunday Schools, or SSS, carry a liberal hue. On the one hand, they oppose the church, and on the other hand, they oppose anti-socialist parties, while at the same time not associating with socialists. Currently, they have 6,420 students and 109 schools throughout the UK, and undoubtedly, it is developing.

What is their attitude towards religion? The secretary-general of the SSS once said the following:

"...Whether there is a God or not, we do not know. Therefore, we have no right to educate children about things we do not know. Therefore, we do not educate about the afterlife; what we do teach children is to live in accordance with their principles, that is, to educate them on how to strive for socialism as adults..."

Since the SSS rejects the doctrines of the church, what do they use as their belief? Interestingly, they also use ten principles to replace the Ten Commandments of the church, which are stipulated to be recited by children every Sunday. Two of the ten principles are worth mentioning, namely:

"In order to discover the truth, one must observe and think, not believe in things that conflict with reason, and not deceive oneself or others."

"We are based on...justice...to help create a new society!"

It can be said directly that the education of the SSS is not to force children to bury themselves in socialist theories dogmatically, but to enable them to correctly understand everything through their own observation and understanding.

Regarding the principles of the SSS movement, many are indeed correct, but many are also trapped in a deep quagmire of humanitarianism. For example, at one SSS meeting, there was the following opinion:

"Love is more powerful than hatred. And a person wanting to shake another person's hand is more powerful than extending it in contempt. The most powerful thing in the world is where people have reverence. Therefore, people should revere mothers, fathers, children, the sympathy and mutual love of friends. The sympathy and mutual love of mothers, fathers, children, and friends is the ultimate powerful victory."

This theory not only violates the ten principles of the SSS, but also risks creating a new religion. This theory is clearly incorrect, because children's concept of "love" can be said to be innate, and the cultivation of this concept lies in the social environment. If we do not actively transform the social environment, but simply promote idealistic "love," it is useless. Under this capitalist social system, so-called "universal love" is just an empty and pleasant term; in fact, imperialism will never love weak nations, and exploiters will never love the exploited. Therefore, although we want to love our enemies and not hate them, it is both unreasonable and impossible!

Amateur Art

"The Question of Saving the Nation Through Music"

— Shi Ru Yu

After the September 18th Incident, common "national salvation" proposals included "saving the nation by boycotting goods," "saving the nation through aviation," "saving the nation through education," "saving the nation through motors," "saving the nation through lottery tickets," and so on. There were also "saving the nation by dancing" and "saving the nation by civil war," simply too many to list. Now, some people are advocating "saving the nation through music." But to sum it up in one sentence, their original intentions are all patriotic. One gentleman, advocating "saving the nation through music," said this: "What kind of powerful stimulant is needed to save a nation mired in decline? To be honest, only 'music' can save China." He went on to say: "Indeed, we deeply feel that decadent and uninspired China is indeed lacking the infusion of art." Yes, we admit that China is indeed lacking the infusion of art, especially the common knowledge of "music" is even more childish. However, the reason why the Chinese nation has reached this state of decline and decadence is not merely because of a lack of artistic infusion, but there are even greater reasons, such as the misuse of terms like "enduring humiliation and bearing heavy burdens"...etc. Now, I would like to put forward a few points regarding the idea of "saving the nation through music" for discussion with everyone.

The emergence and development of every art form has its social background. For example, European and American countries are the most developed capitalist countries, coupled with the prosperity of science and the extreme attainment of material enjoyment, so their art is naturally advanced. However, despite the progress, it is undeniable that it remains an enjoyment for a minority of leisured people. As for colonial China, it goes without saying that it has been struggling and suffering from natural disasters, man-made disasters, foreign aggression, and civil wars for years. Most people cannot even secure their basic living needs, so how can they care about art that cannot feed the hungry or clothe the cold? Indeed, we need to look further afield and see what is the reason why the people of European and American countries are so lively and dignified? Is it because their music is particularly developed? I say, it is because their lives are relatively affluent and stable, hence their liveliness. The rich always seem dignified in the eyes of the poor. But let's look further afield, as a result of capitalism developing to its extreme, the whole world is in a great depression, making the poor increase day by day, and the situation is very different from before.

Speaking of the creation of art, the first condition is ample leisure time, followed by economic power. Please look at the 400 million people in China, how many are free from worries about food and clothing and have ample economic ability? That's just a few young masters and ladies from wealthy families. However, they spend their days hidden in an ivory tower, oblivious to the world, enjoying themselves, how would they know how many tens of thousands of subjugated slaves in the Northeast are being slaughtered by imperialists, and how many innocent people are being devoured by floods and droughts? But sometimes, when they are happy, when they are bored, they also want to find some opportunities to show off. I remember a few months ago, someone waved the banner of saving the nation through art and opened a painting exhibition. However, as a result, many paintings were sold, but the country was not saved. The facts are right in front of us, the position of Japanese imperialists in the Northeast is becoming more and more consolidated, and the most...again...are thinking about...This is hardly the time to be enjoying music?

The proponents of saving the nation through music say that Western violins and pianos are derived from Chinese musical instruments. Our national character, which is good at imitation but lacks creativity, has made us abandon national music and imitate Western music. Now, music (along with other arts) has become a pastime for a few people. However, aren't the cheap musical instruments of our own country also owned by a minority of the leisured class? Basically, a person who is oppressed by life will not spend money to buy musical instruments, and also has no time to study music.

We must know that the distress of groups of young men and women is definitely not just because they lack the comfort and stimulation of music. Aren't radios and gramophones all over the streets transmitting all kinds of songs? We have quite a few powerful stimulants! However, to a large group of unemployed, suffering children, hearing this kind of decadent commercial music will only increase their troubles and touch their sadness, because the wounds in their hearts can only be healed by work and bread. Then, perhaps only music like the French Marseillaise can move their cold hearts? However, what most of the people in France lack is bread, not music.

Small Social Model

Slum Workers' Train: Flesh Barrier

— Zhang Cheng Liang

Train No. XX from S Port to N City. No first class, no second class, not even the usual third class. It's a bluish-gray, covered in coal ash, never washed, "slum workers' train"—such a long train, with a gloomy face, leaning lazily against platform X. A surging tide of people is agitated on the platform.

The engine is reluctantly panting in front, its nose pointing to the sky, its heart is hot, the blood is rushing. It will run away, as long as someone hits it on the head with a whip. Hit it with a whip, a whip, a whip... Damn it! Look at the railway police. They are standing at the ticket booth, blindly pushing people.

"Damn it, it's infuriating to buy a ticket, getting whipped. The guy at the ticket booth is even more arrogant, not accepting small silver coins, insisting on large silver dollars to make change, isn't he just trying to skim off the top! One dollar and thirty-five cents, gave him two silver dollars, only changed six small silver coins. Humph! Bullying the poor doesn't make you a hero."

"What are you fussing about? 'Spending money to get angry' is a common saying, there's no way around it if you want to ride his train."

The platform is extremely long, the train is extremely long, and people are surging like a tide. Thin yellow faces, bald heads and heads with long messy hair, not a single intact garment, not a hint of cheerful emotion, children lying on the backs of dirty women, crying and demanding to be squeezed to the front where their fathers are. The fathers, however, turn their faces back to scold the women: "So polite! Squeeze harder, can't you see? The train is packed."

Packed full, running towards the engine, there isn't a single carriage that's relatively empty. Dark heads swaying restlessly in the carriage windows. Puffs of roast duck smell, bursts of thick smoke that block the sunlight.

"Let's just get on this carriage!"

The carriage steps seem to be deliberately making things difficult for people, without any curvature. Hanging onto that iron bar to climb up, a careless step and you'll slip under the train, look at those single women, it's hard enough for them! It's even more dangerous with children—this is the "slum workers' train."

"Slum workers' train," you haven't seen the situation inside the carriage yet. The stench of fish and rot fills the air. Rotten, bloody legs without socks. Heads with external sores, dripping with pus. Anxious, expressionless faces of men and women, covered by a layer of coal smoke, covered by noisy conversations, here, everyone is being expelled from the city after suffering from the thorns of life. There is no cheerful emotion, no seeds of hope, and even less comfortable air, everything is deeply trapped in a sorrowful abyss.

However, looking out from the carriage window, the street scenes of the city are still joyous.

Four narrow hard benches, with four "flesh barriers" sitting on them. Those old women, women, and children who couldn't find seats later sat on the floor, their legs bumping into heads, their heads resting on legs, the toilet is also crowded with four or five people, a few young people have climbed onto the luggage racks, if it gets any more crowded, the carriage will break.

"Might as well break the carriage, at least let us get a breath of fresh air."

You know, there are only a few window holes in a slum workers' train, letting darkness accompany the stifling air. Some infectious germs are spreading in the stifling air. The smell of inferior cigarettes permeates the air. People who have been in prison would not feel any painful aversion here.

"Hey! Trying to die? Pig!" The railway police whipped the old man who was hanging on the carriage steps trying to relieve himself, and cursed him with this sentence, as the train was already crawling away.
