Amateur Coffee Shop

"Amateur" Without "Spare Time"

— Qiu Jin Xian

Recently, the word "amateur" has become very popular. Because the "amateur" is all the rage, so there are many wonderful words, such as "amateur tutoring", "amateur sports", "amateur entertainment", countless, so anyone seems to be able to fully use the spare time to things that are beneficial to the body and mind. But, right on top of this, there have been some small problems: First, we must first understand whether every employee has "spare time" to use? Taking Shanghai as an example, apart from the "employees" of institutions, foreign firms, and modern shops, there is no so-called "spare time" at all, and employees without "spare time" probably account for more than 70% of all employees in the city. These employees who do not have "spare time" happen to be knowledge-hungry. Their work and life, taking shop assistants as an example, generally start from 7:00 in the morning and continue to work until 9:00 or 10:00 in the evening. Within this twelve or thirteen hours of working time, apart from those times when they can sit down for a moment to eat (if there are no customers), it is best to keep their hands and feet moving all day long. Even if there are no customers, they must use a feather duster to wipe and dust, to show diligence, lest the employer ask you to "seek a better position elsewhere". Therefore, even when they need to relieve themselves, they have to hurry up, let alone hold books and newspapers to study. By the time they put up the shutters at nine or ten o'clock, they are already so tired that they don't know what they are doing, and they practice their "amateur sleep", who still has the energy to engage in "tutoring", "sports", "entertainment",...etc.?

Taking workers as an example, their lives are even worse than shop assistants. They enter the factory at six o'clock in the morning, fight the man-eating machines until six or seven o'clock in the evening, go home with their heads drooping and their spirits down, and have to "bury the pot and make rice" to fill their five internal organs temple. They leave the cold rice for tomorrow to take into the factory, and fill half their stomach with the leftovers. Then, they peel off the dirty clothes that are so dirty that they don't know what they are and are full of the smell of machine oil, and wash them vigorously. After finishing this work, it can naturally be regarded as "spare time", but if they delay for a while to do some "tutoring", "sports", "entertainment",... they will surely hear echoes in the factory tomorrow, you are still snoring, and you have lost a day's work, and you are going hungry for a day.

Therefore, the so-called "spare time" is still something that only employees in the middle and upper levels have the right to enjoy. The more urgently the lower-level employees need to use their spare time to increase their knowledge and health, the more they can only stand at the bottom of hell, cran their necks, and wait for the bosses to automatically improve the unreasonable treatment of their young partners and workers under their rule when the sun rises in the west.

Now let's study the middle and upper-level employees who have the right to enjoy "spare time". Taking myself as an example, although my working hours are only six hours between 9:00 AM and 12:00 PM, and 2:00 PM and 5:00 PM, but when I get up early, I have to take care of the children, let my wife go to buy groceries, and after lunch, I have to take care of the children again, let my wife tidy things up, and after finishing my official duties in the afternoon, I have to take care of the children again, let my wife do the laundry. After eating dinner, I have to write some articles to exchange for some money to supplement the household expenses. Naturally, my life cannot represent the average person, but undoubtedly, there must be many employees in the same layer as me who live the same life as me,——although they have "spare time", but in fact, there is no opportunity to use it to temper their body and mind.

From this, we can find a conclusion, all "amateur" sports, shop assistants in old-style shops, workers selling labor, although they have spare time, are unable to enjoy it because they are plagued by poverty and family burdens. In fact, the lowest level of people who can fully use their spare time for "amateur XX" are still the people in the petty bourgeoisie, and the children of the people in the petty bourgeoisie.

Under the deformed social and economic organization, such a deformed product is naturally inevitable. But culture is progressing with the giant wheels of the times, and I always hope that in the near future, there will no longer be anyone in this world who is a "spare time" outsider.
